3. **Pro bono criminal defense** — a deliberate proportion, calibrated to her own metric of vocational integrity. Cases are screened for fit; she does not take what she cannot serve.

She is current with her bar dues, in good standing, has not been the subject of a disciplinary complaint in the recent era (a meaningful change from the Slott period, when professional discipline was a recurring stressor), and is increasingly cited in the legal press as the practical authority on her niche. She has been invited to teach a seminar at one of the New York law schools and has, on the available evidence, declined — consistent with a stated preference for practice over pedagogy and an unstated preference for keeping her cognitive bandwidth on her cases and her recovery.

She courts as Jennifer, by default. This is a substantial change. Pre-trauma, the choice of form for court appearances was contested and humiliating; post-trauma, the human form is no longer experienced as a humiliation to be endured but as a body she lives in. The dysphoric quality has not vanished — observers who know her well can still read the small physical tells of the form-discomfort (the slight habitual touch to the side of the neck when seated; the way she resettles her shoulders before standing to argue) — but the affect has dropped from acute to manageable background.

## 4.5 The Transformation in Its Current Use

The most clinically significant somatic datum of the current era is the changed relationship to the gamma form. She transforms now: (a) deliberately, with conscious intent; (b) for defined purposes, usually heroic or protective; (c) with a brief preparatory ritual that did not exist pre-trauma — a measurable pause, a breath sequence, a settling. The hulk-outs of the Tamaki period, gray-coded and rage-driven and ego-dystonic, are no longer the default. The green form has been recovered.

But it has not been recovered as it was. The pre-trauma She-Hulk was a release; the current She-Hulk is a tool. The pre-trauma transformation was the more comfortable home; the current transformation is a deliberate occupation of an instrument she trusts again, conditionally. She emerges from it now with a brief decompression period — she sits, she drinks water, she does not immediately resume normal social interaction — that pre-trauma Jennifer did not need. The form has been re-integrated; the easy seamlessness has not been restored, and on the available evidence will not be.

Combat tempo: lower. She is not currently rostered to a full-time team. She does ad-hoc Avengers reserve work, occasional consult to the FF on legal-adjacent metahuman crises, and has been observed in two-to-three engagements in the published period that required full transformation. Recovery between engagements is longer than her pre-trauma curve. This may be partially endocrine (she is in her late twenties, biologically; the metabolic cost of full transformation is non-trivial) but is primarily psychological pacing. She is managing her own exposure.

## 4.6 Mental Health Status: Current Picture

The therapeutic relationship initiated during the Tamaki period has been maintained, at a reduced cadence — from weekly to roughly biweekly, with availability for unscheduled contact during stressors. This is the clinically appropriate maintenance pattern for a person in the late phase of trauma recovery.

PTSD criteria, current standing: subthreshold. She no longer meets full criteria. Residual features: occasional sleep disturbance under stress, hypervigilance in crowds that resembles the pre-trauma pattern but with a measurably longer recovery, mild intrusive imagery on anniversaries and specific triggers (Hawkeye sightings, gamma-related news), and a persistent low-grade survivor cognition around Bruce that surfaces in dreams and in unguarded moments. Panic episodes: rare, not abolished, manageable when they occur. She has the toolkit.

Substance use: significantly reduced from the Slott-era pattern. Social drinking only, at lower frequency and lower volume. The behavioral function — using intoxication to access permission for desire — has been substantially defused by the work she has done on the underlying schema. She does not need the chemical permission as often because she has begun to grant it to herself.

Grief: the Banner loss is integrated but not closed and will not close. She has reached the configuration in which the grief is a feature of the landscape rather than the weather. Bruce's various subsequent returns and re-deaths in the published record have, on inference, been complicated for her in ways the file would expect — each return reopens the cardiac wound, each re-death reseals it imperfectly. She has reportedly maintained selective contact during his return periods and selective withdrawal during the death-state intervals, which is the adaptive pattern.

## 4.7 The Father Question, Current

William Morris Walters remains a load-bearing absence. The file has no record of substantial reconciliation. Contact is reportedly minimal, formal, and initiated by neither party with any frequency. The subject has not, on the available evidence, done the direct relational work with her father that she has done with herself; she has instead done the work that makes the father-wound less acutely operative without requiring his participation. This is, in clinical terms, an acceptable resolution — one does not need the original injuring party to participate in one's recovery — but it leaves the schema permanently present as a vulnerability rather than abolished.

Operational implication: father-figure transferences (judges, senior partners, older male authority figures in superhuman institutions) remain a live pressure point and should be flagged in any predictive model of her behavior under institutional stress.

## 4.8 Social Configuration, Present

**Inner ring (daily/weekly contact, full disclosure):** Jack Hart (domestic partner); Patsy Walker (closest peer friend, trauma-era bonded); her current therapist (professional but load-bearing); her paralegal of long standing (vocational intimate, knows the practice and the person).

**Second ring (regular contact, partial disclosure):** Louise Mason (reactivated); Wyatt Wingfoot (re-friended after the romantic chapter closed cleanly, a non-trivial achievement); selected Avengers and FF members on a per-case basis; the small circle of attorneys nationally who can practice in her niche.

**Third ring (functional contact):** Clients, opposing counsel she respects, the metahuman policy community, several of the younger heroes she has informally mentored.

**Cold/dormant:** GLK&H principals (the firm relationship ended cleanly but is not warm); a number of pre-trauma social acquaintances she has not chosen to reactivate; the LA-period network almost entirely; her father.

The configuration is leaner than her pre-trauma social map, more deliberate, and more sustainable. She has stopped trying to be available to everyone. This is, again, the trauma-work showing in the architecture.

## 4.9 Current Daily Pattern (Inferred from Behavioral Record)

Mornings begin early; she is a habitual early riser, and the post-trauma sleep architecture has reinforced this rather than disrupted it (early waking is part of the residual hyperarousal, repurposed into productive time). A brief physical practice — stretching, light cardio, never to exhaustion in human form. Coffee, dark, no ritual fuss. She reads the legal press and one general newspaper before email.

Office by 8:30, typically. She prefers in-person work but has maintained the remote-capable infrastructure she built during the trauma period when leaving the apartment was hard. Court days run on the standard schedule; non-court days are blocked into deep-work intervals with deliberate breaks. She eats lunch, which her pre-trauma self did inconsistently. She leaves the office on time more often than not — another change.

Evenings vary. Jack is home some nights and contained others. She cooks more than she did pre-trauma. The apartment is calm. She reads, she watches things, she sees Patsy or one or two others once or twice a week. She is in bed by a reasonable hour and on bad nights uses the sleep-hygiene protocols her therapist taught her.

Weekends: protected. Pre-trauma Jennifer worked weekends as a default; current Jennifer does not, except under genuine necessity. The boundary is held.

This is, by the standards of any prior era of her file, an almost startlingly regulated life. The party-girl pattern of the mid-2000s is fully extinct. The crisis-driven schedule of the Avengers/FF prime years is gone. What remains is a woman in her late twenties (biologically; older in lived time and trauma age) who has built, by deliberate construction, a sustainable existence.

## 4.10 Current State: Summary Assessment

The subject is, at the moment of this dossier section, in the most psychologically integrated condition of her recorded life. This is not the same as the most comfortable condition of her recorded life — the easy gamma-form confidence of the mid-period is gone and will not return — but integration and comfort are different goods, and she has chosen the deeper one.

The split between the human and transformed self-representations, which was the central psychological fact of her existence for thirty years, has been substantially metabolized. She is not two selves managing a bifurcation; she is one self that has two bodies available to it, with adult judgment about which to deploy. The Jennifer-form is no longer a humiliation; the She-Hulk-form is no longer a refuge. Both are her.

The relational pattern has shifted measurably. She is in a partnership she has not exited. The friendships are fewer and closer. The professional life is calibrated to the person rather than to the persona.

The vulnerabilities are unchanged in structure but reduced in operational intensity: the father-wound, the Bruce-grief, the small-girl schema, the sexual-agency tripwire. These are permanent features. She has not been cured of being herself; she has become more capable of being herself without being capsized by it.

Predictive note for the file: the subject is currently in a stable configuration that has not yet been tested by a major destabilizing event of the magnitude of Civil War II. The reasonable inference, based on the demonstrated capacity for trauma work and the strengthened support architecture, is that she would survive such a test better than she survived the last one. The unreasonable confidence — that she would survive it without serious reorganization — is not warranted. She is well. She is not invulnerable. The dossier records both.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## SECTION: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled from longitudinal review of clinical inference, observed somatic behavior, and forty-plus years of recorded incident. This section maps the body — every injury, every transformation, every substance, every surgery the body did not need and the surgeries the body refused — and the psychological tax each event levied.*

---

### I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE (PRE-INCIDENT, c. ages 0–24)

**Anthropometrics, pre-transformation adult baseline.** Height 5'10" (a fact she has consistently understated to interlocutors throughout her twenties — file note: the understatement is the tell; tall girls who shrink the number have been told their height is a problem by someone whose opinion mattered). Weight in the 135–145 lb range across her law-school years, lean-mesomorph build, long femur, narrow shoulder relative to hip, low resting heart rate (jogger's bradycardia, mid-50s), blood pressure consistently normotensive in the 108/68 range. Right-hand dominant. Eyes green (uncorrected to 20/20 with mild astigmatism, OS worse than OD — reading glasses by 26, used in chambers, never in court). Hair brunette, density average, worn long since adolescence with a brief and immediately regretted shoulder-length cut at 19 (the regret itself is data: the hair is a curtain she keeps available).

**Childhood medical timeline.** Unremarkable infancy. Standard immunization schedule per LA County records of the period. Chickenpox at six (faint residual scar, left supraorbital ridge, visible only at close range). Tonsillectomy at eight (recovery longer than typical; she was eating popsicles alone in a hospital room while the Sheriff worked — she has never told this story but it is in the discharge notes). One greenstick fracture, right radius, age nine, falling from a tree she was not supposed to be in. One fractured incisor, age eleven, bicycle accident; the tooth was crowned, the crown is visible only on dental imaging. Menarche at twelve, cycle regular, dysmenorrhea moderate, managed with OTC analgesics; no hormonal contraception until law school. Reported recurrent tension-type headaches throughout high school, frontal-occipital band distribution, with onset clustered around exam weeks and home conflict; never formally diagnosed, never treated.

**The car accident, age c. 8.** No skeletal injury of clinical significance documented in the surviving emergency record; soft-tissue contusion, seatbelt sign across the right clavicle, transient post-traumatic confusion. The mother died at the scene. *The body remembers this in ways the bones do not.* Subject has, into adulthood, a documentable startle response to the specific sound profile of a tire skid on dry pavement, an unconscious tightening of the right shoulder when she reaches for a seatbelt (the rotator on that side runs marginally tighter than the left), and a lifelong aversion to riding in the front passenger seat that she rationalizes as motion sickness. There is no motion sickness. There is a child in a wreck next to her dead mother. The somatic engram is permanent and was never given clinical attention because the household did not do clinical attention.

**Adolescent and college baseline.** No surgeries, no hospitalizations, no chronic illness. One sprained ankle (intramural soccer, UCLA). Episodic insomnia, sleep-onset type, throughout undergraduate and law school, self-medicated with herbal tea and late-night reading rather than pharmacology. Occasional social alcohol, two-drink ceiling, no documented intoxication episodes through 24. No drug use of record. No sexual-health concerns of record; routine gynecological care, normal. One asymptomatic ovarian functional cyst noted incidentally on imaging at 23, resolved without intervention.

**The pre-incident body, then, in summary:** healthy, intact, athletic in a recreational rather than competitive register, unremarkable to a clinician, and carrying invisibly a single deep traumatic engram around the loss of the mother and a low-grade stress-mediated somatic pattern (headaches, insomnia, shoulder asymmetry) consistent with chronic adaptation to a critical paternal environment. *She walked into the apartment the day of the shooting with a body that had been bruised mostly on the inside.*

---

### II. THE INDEX EVENT — PENETRATING TRAUMA AND THE TRANSFUSION

**Mechanism.** Multiple gunshot wounds, torso, delivered by Trask-affiliated shooters at her residence. Best reconstruction from canon: at minimum two penetrating wounds, one through the left upper quadrant (probable splenic involvement, certain volume loss), one through-and-through to the right flank. Blood loss catastrophic. Pre-hospital exsanguination state — by the time Banner reached her, she was Class IV hemorrhagic shock: tachycardia decompensating to bradycardia, narrowing pulse pressure, mottling, depressed sensorium, agonal respiration. Survival probability under any conventional protocol: zero, or close enough that the distinction is academic.

**The transfusion.** A field transfusion, donor-to-recipient, no cross-match, no typing, no anticoagulant, no volume metering, executed by a non-surgeon under acute distress. By any rational metric the procedure should have killed her three times over: hemolytic transfusion reaction (ABO mismatch probability ~64% in random pairing — though Banner is family, raising the probability of compatibility), bacterial contamination, air embolism, citrate toxicity (moot, no anticoagulant), volume insufficient to restore perfusion, the donor blood itself a known mutagenic agent of unknown dose. *It worked.* The gamma-saturated erythrocytes did not merely replace volume; they reconstructed.

**Acute somatic sequelae of the transfusion.** Fever spike to ~104°F in the first six hours per emergent observation, generalized myalgia, transient pigmentary shift (the first hint of green at the IV sites, fading), grip-strength elevation noted by the second day to roughly twice baseline before stabilizing pre-transformation, accelerated wound closure (the GSW tracks were granulating at a rate observed in burn-unit pediatric cases, not adult trauma), and — the most psychologically loaded acute finding — a sensation she has described in several interviews and depositions as *"the room getting smaller."* That is interoceptive: her body was expanding its sense of itself before the visible transformation began.

**Psychological impact of the index event.** Three simultaneous insults:
1. *Assault and near-death.* She was shot in her home, by men she had not personally wronged, because of a client. This permanently inflected her relationship to her own practice: she has, ever since, conducted threat-assessment of every client engagement at a level her colleagues find excessive and that she experiences as ordinary professional hygiene. She does not sit with her back to a door. She knows where the exits are in every restaurant. This is not pathology; this is calibrated. *The body learned that the work could come find her at home.*
2. *Survival as gift from the cousin.* Banner saved her life with his own blood. This act welded her affection for him into something closer to indebtedness-as-love — and made his eventual death, decades later, a wound that touched the original wound of the transfusion itself. *His blood was in her. When he died, something in her bled.*
3. *The discovery, immediately, that the transformation was pleasurable.* This is the divergence point from her cousin and the founding fact of the Walters psychology. She did not experience the gamma incident as curse, contamination, or violation. She experienced it as *enlargement.* Within days she was hunting her would-be killers, and the hunt felt good. The clinical significance: a person whose pre-morbid baseline included a deep, unmetabolized smallness encountered an exogenous intervention that made her, literally, large — and the experience was met by a self-system that had been waiting for it. The transfusion did not just give her a second body. It revealed which body she had always wanted.

---

### III. THE GAMMA MUTATION — CHRONIC ACQUIRED CONDITION

**Phenotype, transformed state.** Height 6'7" (a 9-inch gain, mostly trunk and lower extremity). Weight approximately 700 lb (a fivefold increase, distributed as muscle mass with negligible adipose). Skin pigmentation shifted to a distinctive green, hair color preserved (a small but psychologically interesting fact: the brunette persists; the self-signifier she carries on her head does not surrender to the mutation). Eye color preserved. Voice marginally lower in fundamental frequency but recognizable, retaining her cadence and verbal idiosyncrasies. Strength class: superhuman, low end of Class 75–100 at baseline, ascending with sustained exertion and emotional load. Durability: small-arms fire substantially deflected, intermediate calibers cause superficial bruising, high-caliber and exotic-ordnance can wound; healing rates approximately 40–100x normal.

**Cognition in transformed state.** *No IQ loss.* This is the single most important clinical fact in the file after the index event itself. Where her cousin loses prefrontal regulation, Walters retains every cognitive function — verbal fluency, working memory, executive control, theory of mind, abstract reasoning. She has tried complex cases in transformed state. She has drafted appellate briefs in transformed state. The gamma mutation is, in her, almost entirely somatic. *She gets the body without paying the mind-tax.* The psychological implication is large: she was never forced, the way her cousin was, to externalize the transformation as a monster who is not her. She had to integrate it as her, because cognitively it always was her.

**Voluntariness, evolving.** Early phase (Savage She-Hulk era): involuntary, stress-triggered, threshold roughly correlated with sympathetic arousal — anger, fear, sexual excitement, adrenal-loaded combat states. Trigger latency seconds. Reversion latency variable, often requiring sleep or reduction of arousal. Mid-phase (post-Avengers tenure through mid-2000s): fully voluntary, near-instantaneous, with the form essentially permanent by election. Late phase (post-Civil War II): voluntariness compromised; transformation re-acquired an involuntary, intrusive quality under acute affect, with the resulting form qualitatively altered (see §V).

**Reproductive and endocrine considerations.** The most underexamined chapter of her medical record. Gamma physiology and human gestation are, as the canon obliquely treats it, incompatible at the cellular level: the transformed metabolic envelope is incompatible with embryonic development; the human form's reproductive machinery functions but is shadowed by the integrated gamma genome in ways no one has fully characterized. The Slott-era pregnancy storyline and the periodic, oblique grief she has expressed in private contexts (and once on the record, briefly, in a conversation with Patsy Walker) point to a settled internal understanding that biological motherhood is, for her, foreclosed. *She does not bring this up. She does not need to. The file notes that she has, across forty years, never once held another person's infant on-panel without a particular set of her jaw that lasts about a second too long.*

**Menstrual cycle, post-mutation.** Cycle in human form remains regular. Cycle in transformed state is, per inference, suppressed or substantially altered — the metabolic envelope of the 700-lb form does not support standard endometrial physiology. Subject has reported (off-record, to a treating clinician in the Tamaki-era therapy) that the body in either form is "honest" about which one she is in, and that switching forms across a cycle produces interoceptive confusion she has learned to ignore.

**Aging.** Apparent biological aging in both forms is markedly slowed relative to chronologic age. Subject presents as late-20s across publication despite forty-plus years of elapsed narrative time. The mechanism is presumed gamma-cellular and is the same metabolic phenomenon that prevents true addiction biology. *Functional immortality, or near it, has not been clinically discussed with her and is not a topic she raises.* It is, however, almost certainly a background psychological pressure: she has watched non-gamma friends and colleagues age in ways she does not, and the social fact of this is metabolized through humor she does not always bring all the way to the surface.

---

### IV. INJURY LEDGER

A non-exhaustive but representative inventory, chronologic where possible:

- **GSW, index event** (above). Full recovery. Residual: zero visible scarring on transformed body; on human body, faint stellate hypopigmentation at entry sites, palpable only, not visible without close inspection. She is aware of them. She touches them, unconsciously, when nervous — left upper quadrant, two-finger press, three to five seconds, during stressful deposition prep. *Tell.*
- **Multiple blunt-force traumas, Avengers tenure.** Concussions inferred from numerous impacts; gamma-mediated neuroprotection presumed. No documented post-concussive syndrome.
- **Penetrating trauma, FF tenure.** Multiple, including cosmic-energy burns (Galactus-adjacent engagements), Skrull-related wounds, dimensional-displacement injuries. All resolved without sequelae.
- **Crush injuries, multiple.** Notable: a bus-impact event, mid-1980s, full healing within hours. The bone-density of the transformed form is such that fractures require energies orders of magnitude above the human pain threshold; the subjective experience of pain is preserved at appropriate scale.
- **Power loss episodes.** The Fantastic Four's deliberate suppression of her transformation (Slott era) was, in clinical terms, an iatrogenic injury inflicted by people she trusted, ostensibly therapeutically. Subject experienced this as betrayal and as forced regression. The somatic experience of being returned to the human body against her will produced an acute dysphoric reaction, sleep disturbance, and a several-week period of compromised functioning. *The relevant medical concept is not "depowered." The relevant medical concept is "involuntary detransition of a chosen embodied state."* The file treats it as such.
- **Cardiac arrest, Civil War II.** *The clinical event of her adult life.* Thanos-inflicted blunt trauma of cosmic magnitude. Confirmed asystole. Resuscitation by Avengers medical with gamma-aware protocols. Down-time long enough that anoxic injury is plausible; preserved cognition on recovery suggests gamma-mediated neuroprotection again, but the subjective experience of having died was not neuroprotected against. She remembers it. She has described, in therapy, a darkness with no edges and no time. *She has not flown commercial since.*
- **Repeated soft-tissue injuries during Tamaki-era loss-of-control episodes,** mostly self-inflicted during transformations she did not initiate — abrasions, contusions, several lacerations from breaking through her own apartment walls. Healed without scar; the apartment did not.
- **No documented amputation, no organ resection, no transplant, no implanted device.** Her body is, surgically, virgin. Surgeons cannot operate on her in the transformed state (instrumentation fails), and in the human state she has not required intervention. *She has never been opened up.* This is itself psychologically relevant: she has avoided the experience of medical helplessness that her cousin has been subjected to repeatedly, and the asymmetry quietly informs her sense of the family's gamma legacy.

---

### V. THE POST-CWII SOMATIC RECONFIGURATION

The trauma of Civil War II did not merely produce a psychiatric syndrome (see §4 of the master file). It produced an *altered phenotype.* The transformation she had owned for thirty years began presenting differently:

- **Color and morphology shift.** The form trended toward larger, grayer, more morphologically Hulk-like under high-affect trigger — closer to her cousin's earlier gray presentation than to her established green. The subjective report: she did not recognize herself in mirrors during these episodes.
- **Cognitive narrowing in the altered state.** The mind-tax she had never paid began, partially, to come due. Not full cognitive collapse, but compressed affective range — rage-dominant, language reduced, social cognition impaired. This is the first and only time in her medical history that the gamma form has presented as ego-dystonic.
- **Hyperarousal and threshold collapse.** Trigger threshold dropped precipitously; transformations occurred during sleep, during sexual activity, during ordinary conversation. The sense of bodily sovereignty she had built her adult identity around was, for the first time, in question.
- **Somatic flashback.** Re-experiencing the cardiac arrest as a chest pressure, breath-holding, and a peculiar interoceptive certainty of dying — episodes lasting seconds to minutes, occurring without external trigger.

**The clinical recovery arc.** Therapy, explicit and on-record. Pharmacology (not specified in canon, but inferred SSRI trial consistent with presentation; her gamma metabolism likely required atypical dosing). Behavioral exposure to the transformation, gradient. Reconstruction of social contact. By the Rowell-era recovery, the form is reintegrated, the cognitive preservation in transformed state restored, and the trigger threshold returned to voluntary control — *but the easy possession of the body is gone.* She now lives in the gamma form with the same conscious awareness that a recovered patient lives in any body that has betrayed them once. *The miracle is no longer taken for granted. The miracle is something she works at.*

---

### VI. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol.** Episodic heavy use, peaking in the mid-2000s. Behavioral pattern: weekend-loaded, social-context-anchored, content-disinhibitory rather than pure-analgesic — she drinks to access permission for desire, not to numb pain. Gamma metabolism appears to clear ethanol at a rate that prevents either intoxication of clinical depth in the transformed state or true dependence syndrome; she can, in transformed form, consume volumes that would lethally intoxicate a human and present at most as cheerful and slightly less precise. *This is the trap.* The absence of a physiological off-switch means the only governor on her drinking is judgment, and judgment, when she is drinking to gain access to her own appetites, is the thing being deliberately offlined. The behavioral pattern peaked around her most chaotic relational period and tapered with the maturation of her practice and the post-CWII reordering of her life. Current pattern: social, controlled, occasional, conscious.

**Tobacco.** None of record.

**Cannabis.** Inferred occasional, social, unremarkable.

**Other illicit substances.** None of record. She is, by vocation, allergic to losing her bar card; the deterrent is institutional rather than moral.

**Pharmaceuticals.** Sparing. Has refused pain medication on multiple post-injury occasions, citing both gamma metabolism and a preference for unmediated proprioception. Reading-glasses prescription, current. Hormonal contraception, intermittent, discontinued in the post-CWII period and not, per inference, resumed. Possible psychiatric pharmacology during the Tamaki-era treatment (above).

**The chemically-influenced consent episode (Starfox).** This is documented here because the body matters: the affective and behavioral consequences of pheromonal/empathic manipulation are a substance exposure in the relevant sense. Subject's response — sustained legal action, public framing, and a permanent revision of her threat model around empath-class metahumans — is the cleanest available example of her metabolizing somatic violation through her professional frame. *She turned the injury into a case. This is what she does. It is adaptive and it is also a defense.*

---

### VII. THE TWO BODIES — INTEGRATIVE MEDICAL-PSYCHOLOGICAL SUMMARY

The Walters medical file cannot be read as a sequence of conditions. It must be read as the longitudinal record of a person who lives in two bodies and whose entire psychological architecture has been organized around the relationship between them.

The **human body** carries: the dead mother, the disapproving father, the childhood smallness, the tonsillectomy with no one in the chair, the bicycle tooth, the seatbelt sign, the bullet scars. It is the body that was hurt. It is also the body she is required to wear in courtrooms that distrust the other one, and the experience of being made to wear it under compulsion is the closest thing in her clinical record to a sustained dysphoria. *She is not transgender of body, but she is transgender of state* — she has a strong, stable preference for one of her two equally real forms, and being denied access to the preferred form is felt as a violation of identity, not a cosmetic inconvenience.

The **transformed body** carries: the gift of the cousin's blood, the survival, the first-ever experience of being unambiguously seen, agency, desirability, competence, and — since Civil War II — the wound of having been betrayed by the form she most trusted, and the work of having rebuilt that trust.

Neither body is a costume. Neither body is the real one. *They are both her, and the work of her adult life has been learning to be the same person in both.* This is the medical history. Everything else — the GSWs, the cardiac arrest, the alcohol, the reproductive grief, the post-traumatic reconfiguration — is detail in service of that one underlying fact.

She is a woman who was given, by violence and by love and by a cousin's reckless transfusion, a second body. She has spent forty years learning how to live in both. The body, in her case, is the biography.

*— UATU, §2 closes here. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric) for the affective architecture this somatic record carries.*


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## SECTION 6 — SOMATIC ATLAS

A body that has been two bodies for forty years keeps a doubled archive in its tissues. Even in the human form she occupies almost exclusively in professional life, the cellular memory of the larger frame is present — in the way she calibrates space, in the unconscious overshoot of her gestures, in the proprioceptive overcorrection that betrays an operator who has lived at two scales. What follows is the granular record. Every entry below is observed at her baseline human presentation (5'10", lean-athletic, brunette, green-eyed) unless otherwise specified; transformation-state shifts are noted at each subheading where the contrast carries diagnostic weight.

---

### 6.1 Build, Carriage, and Standing Posture

She stands tall — fully tall — which is itself a behavioral datum, because tall women in her cohort statistically slouch by a measurable degree and she does not. The spinal column is held in slight military extension, shoulders set back without strain, sternum forward by perhaps a finger's width past neutral. This is *learned* carriage, not native; it dates from the post-transformation decision to inhabit her physicality on her own terms. Subjects who knew her pre-incident (cousin Banner, the father, early law school cohort) would remember a different girl — shoulders rolled forward, chin tucked, the protective hunch of the small bookish adolescent. That girl is still present in the body's substrate and surfaces under specific stressors (see 6.14).

Weight distribution at rest is biased slightly to the left leg, hip cocked, right knee soft — a courtroom stance she developed early and retains in non-courtroom contexts. When stationary for more than approximately ninety seconds she will shift weight to the opposite leg in a half-conscious cycle; the interval shortens under stress to roughly forty-five seconds.

Hands: at rest standing, typically one hand at the hip (thumb back, fingers forward, a containing posture) and the other free for gesture. She does not cross her arms across the chest in professional settings — she has been trained out of it and has trained herself out of it; the few times it occurs (deposition rooms, hospital waiting areas, her father's house) are diagnostically loud.

**Transformation-state shift:** in She-Hulk form the carriage *relaxes*. The military extension goes; she actually slouches more in the larger body, takes up space casually, leans on door frames, drapes over furniture. This is paradoxical only on the surface: in the gamma form she does not need to perform occupancy of space, because she unambiguously occupies it. The human-form posture is the posture of someone who has to assert a right to her own height.

---

### 6.2 Gait

Stride length in human form is long for her height — approximately 78–82 cm at unhurried pace, which puts her at the upper end for women her stature and forces shorter colleagues to take occasional double-steps to keep up. She is aware of this and modulates it in mentorship contexts (with junior associates, with younger heroes) but not in professional-peer contexts (other partners, opposing counsel, Avengers).

Heel strike is firm; she does not glide. Audible footfall on hard floors at conversational pace. In heels — which she wears in court and at most professional functions, typically a 5–7 cm block heel rather than a stiletto (function over display, but display is not absent) — the strike is even more distinct, and corridor staff at her firms and at courthouses have historically been able to identify her approach by sound alone before she rounds the corner.

Arm swing: moderate, asymmetric. The right arm swings slightly more than the left, consistent with a dominant right side and the lifelong habit of carrying a briefcase or shoulder bag on the left. The left shoulder rides imperceptibly higher as a result — perhaps 4–6 mm — a low-grade structural asymmetry that a physical therapist would flag and that gamma healing periodically resets when she transforms.

**Stress shift:** under moderate stress the gait quickens without lengthening — the cadence accelerates, the stride does not. Under acute stress the heel strike sharpens and she develops a forward lean of perhaps 5°, the body pulled toward the next required action. Under post-traumatic activation (Tamaki-era pattern) the gait collapses entirely: she walks with the shortened, weight-on-the-toes step of someone braced for ambush.

**Transformation-state shift:** in gamma form the gait becomes a *prowl* — longer, looser, more lateral hip rotation, audibly heavier but somehow less hurried. She walks in She-Hulk as though the world has agreed to wait for her, which it largely has.

---

### 6.3 Hands and Manual Habits

Long fingers, well-kept short nails (functional; she has nicked herself on her own keratin during transformation cycles and learned). Nail polish present in approximately 40% of professional appearances — neutrals, clears, occasional dark red in trial weeks (a tell: the dark red is courtroom war paint and predicts a closing argument within 72 hours).

Manual tics:
- **The pen-spin.** Cross or similar weighted pen, rotated between index and middle finger of the right hand in a slow rolling motion during depositions, partner meetings, and any context requiring active listening. Speed of rotation correlates inversely with agreement: faster spin, harder objection coming.
- **The thumb-to-ring-finger press.** Right hand, repeated three to five times in succession, a self-soothing micro-gesture observed in moments of held composure (cross-examination of a witness who is lying, conversations about her father, the Civil War II testimony arc).
- **Hair-tucking.** Right hand, index and middle fingers, tucking a strand of hair behind the right ear. This is the most frequent and diagnostically rich gesture in her repertoire — see 6.5.
- **Document-stacking.** Aligns paper edges compulsively before reading. The stack must be square; she will reach across a conference table to correct an opposing counsel's untidy pile if she is feeling territorial.

She does not bite her nails. She does not pick at cuticles. She does, very occasionally — perhaps once per high-stress day — bring the side of her right thumb to her lower teeth and rest it there for two to four seconds without biting. This is the residual form of a childhood thumb-sucking comfort that her father aggressively trained out of her.

Handshake: firm, dry, full palm engagement, one or two pumps maximum, eye contact held for the duration plus approximately 0.5 seconds after release. She has calibrated this; it is performance and she knows it.

**Transformation-state shift:** in She-Hulk form, fine manual control is preserved (no IQ tax, no fine-motor tax — a critical distinction from Banner), but the gestures *enlarge*. The pen-spin disappears (pens break). The hair-tuck remains, identical in choreography, scaled up. She becomes more tactile with others — a hand on a forearm, a clap on a shoulder — that she would not deploy in human form with the same people. The bigger body permits a friendlier touch register.

---

### 6.4 Face: Resting, Smiling, Listening, Lying

**Resting face** in human form trends serious-neutral with a slight downturn at the mouth corners — the inherited Walters mouth, observed in her father. She has been told her resting face reads as cold or judgmental and has consciously developed a "professional pleasant" overlay (slight upward tension at the corners, soft eye crinkle) for client-facing work. This overlay drops the instant she is alone or thinks she is alone, which security cameras and partners walking in unannounced have repeatedly captured.

**The genuine smile** is asymmetric — left corner rises first and slightly higher, Duchenne markers fully engaged at the eyes, a brief flash of upper teeth. Lasts approximately 1.2–1.8 seconds at full intensity before resolving to a softer holding smile. Provoked reliably by: Banner memories (in safer contexts), good legal craft by an adversary, certain kinds of bad pun, children, dogs.

**The professional smile** is symmetric, eye-engagement minimal, duration controlled. She can hold it indefinitely. Witnesses being cross-examined have described it as the last thing they remember before realizing they had been led somewhere they did not want to go.

**Listening face** is the most distinctive: head tilted approximately 8–12° to the right (almost never left), chin slightly down, eyes on the speaker's mouth as often as their eyes, occasional slow blink at semantic boundaries. She nods sparingly; when she does nod, it means she has logged the point for later use, not that she agrees. Opposing counsel who mistake the nod for assent learn the distinction once.

**Tells when concealing:** she is a trained advocate and an experienced poker face, but baseline tells exist. (1) A 0.3-second compression of the lips before a deliberate misstatement or strategic understatement. (2) The right eyebrow lifts a fraction — perhaps 2 mm — when she is about to ask a question to which she already knows the answer. (3) Under genuine emotional pressure that she refuses to show, the small muscles around the jaw engage and the masseters become briefly visible.

**The eye-roll** is a signature gesture in informal settings — slow, full arc, often paired with a tilt of the head and a half-exhaled laugh. She does not deploy it in court, ever. Its appearance in a setting indicates she has classified the setting as off-duty.

**Transformation-state shift:** in gamma form the facial musculature reads the same expressions at larger scale, but the *threshold* for expression is lower. She-Hulk laughs more easily, frowns more theatrically, lets the face do what the human-form face would suppress. The professional smile largely disappears; She-Hulk does not need it.

---

### 6.5 Hair

Long, dark brunette, naturally wavy with a slight tendency toward frizz in humidity, worn at mid-back length for most of her adult life. Maintenance: professional cut every 6–8 weeks, color refresh (she has a few grays at the temples she chooses to color, vanity acknowledged and owned), deep conditioning weekly. She uses a wide-tooth comb, never a brush on dry hair.

The hair is *load-bearing* psychologically. It is her most consistent vanity and her most reliable self-soothing object. The hair-tuck gesture (right ear, right hand, index and middle fingers, single strand or small section) occurs at minimum 15–25 times per professional day and rises into the 40s on stressful days. Variants:
- **The tuck-and-hold:** the tuck completes and the fingers rest briefly against the side of her neck below the ear. Self-comforting. Common during difficult conversations.
- **The double tuck:** both sides, both hands, simultaneous. Done when consolidating before speaking. A reset.
- **The pull-and-release:** a strand pulled forward over the collarbone, then released. Flirtation register; observed in early stages of romantic interest, also in the controlled deployment of charm against a male judge or juror she has decided to win.
- **The full lift:** both hands, gathering the hair at the nape, lifting it off the neck, holding for 1–3 seconds, releasing. Done when overheated, frustrated, or thinking through a hard problem. The cognitive form of the gesture is the loudest indicator that she is actively reasoning rather than retrieving.

In court the hair is typically pulled back — low bun for trial, half-up for depositions, down for client meetings where humanization is strategic. The decision is made each morning and is itself a small ritual (see 6.13).

**Trauma-era shift:** during the Tamaki-period withdrawal she stopped maintenance entirely for an extended interval — the hair went unwashed for days at a stretch, was tied back without combing, the color went unrefreshed. Hair status is a reliable proxy for her affective regulation.

**Transformation-state shift:** the hair changes color in She-Hulk form to a darker green-black; texture and length are preserved. The hair-tuck gesture survives the transformation unchanged, which is one of the small continuities that proves the same person inhabits both bodies.

---

### 6.6 Eyes and Gaze

Green eyes, slightly cool-toned, with a darker rim at the iris edge. Visual acuity in human form: corrected from mild myopia, contact lenses worn (she keeps a pair of glasses in her desk and another in her go-bag; the glasses come out only in late-night document review and are not deployed publicly — a residual self-image issue traceable to the bookish-girl schema).

**Gaze patterns:**
- **Default conversational:** triangle pattern, left eye / right eye / mouth, dwell times approximately 1.5s / 1.5s / 0.8s, refreshed every 4–6 seconds.
- **Listening to a witness or client:** longer mouth-dwell, scanning for micro-expressions; she has read enough lying faces to do this without conscious effort.
- **Cross-examination:** locked eye contact, blinks suppressed below natural rate, mouth-dwell drops to near zero. This is the predatory mode and it is unmistakable to anyone who has been on the receiving end.
- **Walking into a room:** clockwise scan, exits noted first, then threats, then known faces, then the room's furniture/layout. This is not paranoia; it is operational habit. Avengers training overlaid on attorney training overlaid on the daughter of a sheriff.
- **At rest, alone:** middle-distance defocus with periodic blinks; she reasons with her eyes unfixed.

**Eye-contact under intimacy:** sustained, sometimes uncomfortably so for the partner. She wants to be looked at *while being looked at*. Aversion of gaze in intimacy is a high-confidence signal of avoidance activation (see 6.11).

**Tear pattern:** she does not cry easily and does not cry publicly if she can prevent it. When she does cry, the left eye fills first. She wipes with the side of the index finger, never the back of the hand. Crying jags resolve quickly — she has trained herself to interrupt them — and are followed by approximately 20 minutes of compensatory composure-rebuilding (cold water on the face, hair adjustment, posture reset).

---

### 6.7 Voice and Speech

Mid-alto, resonant, with deliberate diaphragmatic projection developed in trial advocacy training. Speaking rate at baseline approximately 170–185 words per minute — fast, but articulated cleanly; she does not swallow consonants. In closing argument she can drop to 110–130 wpm with extended consonant attack, the slowing itself a rhetorical instrument.

**Vocabulary register shifts** are precisely calibrated:
- Court / formal: full Latinate professional register, complete sentences, no contractions.
- Partner meetings: contractions return, vocabulary remains technical.
- Peer superhuman contexts: rapid colloquial English with profanity used as punctuation, never as content.
- Intimate contexts: voice drops by roughly a third in volume, rate slows by 20%, the register becomes plainer and more declarative.
- With her father: clipped, formal, sentence length shortens, register reverts toward the daughter-form.

**The stammer.** In some childhood accounts she stammered. The stammer is fully extinguished in adult speech under normal conditions but reappears as a brief disfluency — a doubled initial consonant, almost subliminal — under specific high-stress conditions: direct paternal contact, certain conversations about her mother, the immediate aftermath of trauma. It is the most archeological tell in her speech.

**Laugh:** loud, head-back, unselfconscious when genuine. Genuine laugh duration 2–4 seconds; she does not perform extended social laughter. The polite chuckle exists, is recognizable, and is half a tone higher than the real laugh.

**Filler words:** minimal. "Look —" as a turn-opener under pressure. "So" as a structuring particle in argument. She does not say "um"; she pauses instead, which has the additional effect of making interlocutors fill the silence with information she wanted.

**Transformation-state shift:** voice deepens by roughly half an octave in She-Hulk form, projection increases, rate stays the same — same speaker, lower fundamental. The wit registers identically; she is, vocally, more obviously herself in the larger body, not less.

---

### 6.8 Sleep Architecture

Pre-trauma baseline: 6.5–7.5 hours, sleep onset 12–18 minutes, single mid-sleep wake of brief duration, morning rise without alarm by approximately 0615. Sleep position: left side, knees drawn slightly up, right arm across the abdomen, left arm tucked under the pillow. Pillow count: two firm, one body pillow added during high-stress weeks (a substitute presence, observed and self-acknowledged).

Bedroom environmentals: cool (subjectively prefers ~17°C), dark to the point of blackout, white noise machine (she sleeps poorly in true silence — a residual from the cousin-summers when Banner's old fan ran nightly and became sleep-cue). Phone face-down on the nightstand; she has resisted bringing it to bed since the late 2010s.

**Pre-sleep ritual:** read for 20–40 minutes (legal nonfiction, history, occasional fiction — she does not read romance and resents being assumed to), water glass on the nightstand, lights out at a remarkably consistent time give or take trial schedules.

**Dream content (self-reported in therapy, post-CWII):** recurring water/drowning imagery (the mother's accident, refracted); recurring courtroom-without-pants anxiety dreams (career-related); recurring dreams of being unable to transform when she needs to (post-traumatic, persistent). She has reported only one recurring dream of Banner — they are children, fishing, nothing happens — and she values it.

**Post-trauma shift (Tamaki era):** sleep onset extended to 60–90 minutes; multiple mid-sleep wakes; nightmares with motor enactment (she destroyed a headboard in one episode); early morning waking around 0400 with inability to return to sleep. Hypervigilance to ambient sound. She slept on the couch for an extended period — the bedroom had become threat-coded. Recovery trajectory: slow, deliberate, therapy-supported.

**Transformation-state shift:** She-Hulk needs less sleep — 4–5 hours is sufficient — but the metabolic cost of the form during sleep is high enough that she does not sleep transformed by preference. The form sleeps when forced; she does not choose it as a sleep state.

---

### 6.9 Eating and Drinking

**Hunger pattern in human form:** standard. Three meals plus snacks, coffee through the morning, water through the afternoon. She eats *fast* — a habit from law school and never corrected — and is conscious of it in social meals, where she deliberately slows.

**Preferences:** broad, omnivorous, no significant aversions. Strong preference for high-protein breakfasts (eggs, occasionally steak; she will order steak for breakfast in hotels without self-consciousness). Coffee black, two to three cups before 1100, none after 1400. Tea in the evening. She is a competent but uninterested cook — the kitchen is for assembly, not craft — and orders in more than she cooks.

**Restaurants and routes:** she has a small, stable rotation of preferred establishments near each of her professional addresses. Same table when possible. Greets staff by name. Tips at 25% as a moral position.

**Alcohol:** the mid-2000s heavy-use period is documented (§2). Behavioral pattern: wine at dinner shading into spirits at the bar afterward, the second-drink-too-many that lowers the bar to permitting desire. The gamma metabolism prevents physiological addiction but does not prevent the behavioral function. Post-recovery, her use has rebalanced — a glass of wine with dinner, one cocktail at firm events, declines refills. She tracks her own intake unobtrusively.

**Transformation-state shift:** She-Hulk's caloric requirement is enormous — observers have seen her clear three entrees and dessert without affect — and metabolizes alcohol so rapidly that intoxication in the larger form is functionally impossible. This is part of why the human-form drinking carried the affective weight it did: it was the only state in which she could chemically loosen.

---

### 6.10 Grooming and Self-Presentation

**Morning routine, human form, professional day:** shower (10–14 minutes, the longest non-productive interval of her morning, used for cognitive rehearsal), skin care (a multi-step regimen she will not discuss but observably maintains), makeup (medium coverage, defined eye, neutral lip in court, deeper lip outside court), hair (decided per 6.5), wardrobe (decided the night before in trial weeks, decided in the morning otherwise).

**Wardrobe:** professional attire dominates. Suits in dark neutrals (navy, charcoal, black, occasional deep green — she is not unaware of the joke and wears it with intent), shells underneath in jewel tones, a small collection of statement coats. She owns roughly twelve suits in active rotation. Fit is tailored — she pays for tailoring because off-the-rack does not accommodate her shoulders or her height — and the tailoring is conservative enough to read as serious and precise enough to read as expensive. Off-duty: jeans and well-fitted casual wear, the same shoulder-emphasizing cuts in less formal fabrics.

**Jewelry:** minimal. Small earrings (studs in court, slightly more in evening), occasional thin chain necklace, no rings on the working hand. A watch — analog, mid-sized face — on the left wrist, always.

**Scent:** a single signature fragrance worn for years, deployed lightly (one wrist, transferred to the neck), recognizable to those close to her. Switches scents during identity-reset periods (she changed perfumes after the Civil War II recovery — a deliberate olfactory rebooting).

**Nails, skin, teeth:** maintained. The gamma physiology means dental and dermatological problems essentially do not occur; she is a model patient for a dentist who has no work to do.

---

### 6.11 Sexual and Intimate Somatics

A careful subsection, because the file would be incomplete without it and the patterns are diagnostically central.

**Approach behavior:** in active pursuit of a partner, she shifts weight closer (decreasing interpersonal distance by 15–25 cm below social norm), the hair-tuck rate increases, the pull-and-release variant appears, voice drops in volume, laugh becomes more frequent and slightly lower-pitched. Eye contact extends. She touches the partner's forearm or upper arm at conversational accents — brief, calibrated, deniable.

**Initiation:** she initiates. Across forty years of documented relational history the pattern holds: she selects, she signals, she closes the distance. The few exceptions are partners who matched her in directness (Hercules, notably) and she found this matching erotic in itself.

**Intimate state:** the voice change noted in 6.7 is reliable. Breath rate elevates earlier than autonomic baseline would predict — anticipatory. Skin flushes across the chest and throat (vasomotor, visible). Eye contact extended early, sometimes averted later as arousal deepens — the avoidance is not shame but overwhelm, and recovers.

**Post-coital:** she does not, as a rule, sleep next to partners on first or early intimacies. She gets up, drinks water, returns or does not. By the third or fourth night with a partner she has provisionally committed to, she will stay; the change is


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## SECTION 7 — ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

---

### 7.1 The Foundational Template: A Mother Lost, A Father Who Did Not Forgive Her For It

Every adult relational pattern in this subject's life traces, with unusual cleanness, to one specific configuration laid down before age ten: the mother died in a car accident with the daughter in the vehicle, and the father — Sheriff William Morris Walters — either explicitly blamed the child or failed convincingly to disabuse her of the belief that he did. The subject's own retrospective dialogue across multiple eras corroborates the second reading: a paternal silence treated by the child as verdict.

This is the worst possible configuration for the formation of secure attachment. The primary mirroring figure (mother) is suddenly and totally unavailable. The secondary attachment figure (father) is not merely insufficient but presents as actively withholding, and the child reads his withdrawal as causal — *I am why love left this house*. The result is a working model in which:

- **Closeness is dangerous,** because the closest person (mother) was lost.
- **The self is the agent of loss,** because father's grief was channeled as blame.
- **Love must be earned through competence,** because affection-as-given was never the model; affection-as-performance (good grades, good behavior, professional achievement) was the only available currency.
- **Visibility is double-edged:** to be seen is to risk being judged insufficient (father), but to be unseen is to confirm one's own non-existence (mother gone, father turned away).

The subject's adult life is, with remarkable consistency, an attempt to solve this equation. She wants to be *seen accurately and chosen anyway* — a thing her family of origin proved was impossible. Every relationship she enters is, at some level, a re-audition for the role her father refused to confirm.

### 7.2 Attachment Classification: Dismissive-Avoidant with Anxious Substrate

On the Bartholomew four-category model the subject scans as **dismissive-avoidant** in steady state, with a clear **fearful-avoidant** flare under acute relational stress and brief **anxious-preoccupied** episodes early in romantic engagement. She is not securely attached. She does an extremely convincing impression of secure attachment in low-stakes friendship and professional contexts, where the demand for true dependency is low and the rewards of competence are reliable.

The dismissive surface presents as: independence framed as preference, busyness as identity, mobility as freedom, the wit that holds others at conversational arm's length. The anxious substrate presents as: the speed and intensity with which she enters new romantic pairings, the way she organizes her social life around being chosen (the She-Hulk persona is, among other things, an industrial-scale being-chosen mechanism), and the small somatic tells that surface when an attachment figure is unreachable — the checked phone, the re-checked phone, the abandoned book, the second drink.

The fearful component emerges when intimacy crosses a threshold. There is a specific moment, observable in nearly every romantic arc on file, where a partner offers something stable — a domestic question, a future-tense plan, a vulnerability disclosed without performance — and the subject's behavior changes within hours. She exits, picks a fight, takes a case across the country, transforms (or refuses to). The mechanism is not capricious; it is defensive. Real intimacy threatens to activate the unmetabolized maternal-loss / paternal-rejection complex, and the system is built to prevent that activation at almost any cost.

### 7.3 The Bruce Variable

There is exactly one durable, unambiguous, lifelong secure attachment in the file: Robert Bruce Banner. He is the cousin who, during childhood summer visits, was kind to her without requiring performance; who saw the bookish small girl and chose her company; who later, when she was dying on a Los Angeles floor, gave her his blood without calculation. He is the only family member who occupies the attachment-figure role positively.

This is psychologically load-bearing in ways the subject probably under-recognizes consciously and over-feels somatically:

- He is her **proof that one Walters-bloodline relationship can work**. Without him, the data set would be unanimous.
- He is her **gamma-mirror**: the only other person who has lived in two bodies, the only one for whom her central somatic experience requires no translation.
- He is her **ego-ideal in inverted form** — she became what he failed to become (integrated with the transformation), and her competence at it is partly a gift to him, partly a quiet rebuke, partly an offering.
- He is the only person whose **gaze she trusts without preemption**. With Bruce she does not need to perform She-Hulk to be seen, nor perform Jennifer to be safe.

Hawkeye's killing of Bruce in Civil War II is therefore not a discrete bereavement; it is an attachment catastrophe. The one secure base she had — the one relationship the dismissive defense was not deployed against — was extracted from the system, and extracted by an allied hand, which removes even the clean grief of enemy action. The PTSD picture documented in §4 cannot be understood without registering that the trauma is simultaneously *medical* (her own near-death), *relational* (loss of secure base), and *identitarian* (loss of the only other person in the world configured like her).

### 7.4 The Father: The Permanent Open Wound

The Sheriff is the single most consistent relational stressor across forty years of file material. The pattern is invariant:

- **Geographic distance** is maintained whenever the subject has agency over residence. Los Angeles to New York is not a career move; it is an attachment management decision retroactively justified by career.
- **Contact is initiated by external necessity** (a case touching his jurisdiction, a family death, a crisis). She does not call him on holidays without occasion. He does not call her at all in most documented periods.
- **Each contact produces measurable affect dysregulation in the subject within 48 hours** — sleep disturbance, sharper drinking, more aggressive courtroom behavior, increased likelihood of transformation under low provocation.
- **She defends him to others** while criticizing him to herself. This is the classic introject pattern: she has metabolized his disapproval as a voice that lives inside her, and attacks on him from outside feel like attacks on the part of her that still hopes to win him over.
- **Father-transferences are abundant and operationally significant.** Judges, senior partners, certain Avengers (Captain America in particular, until Civil War broke the transference open), her cousin Bruce when he failed her — all draw paternal projection. Her capacity for warm professional respect and her capacity for sudden disproportionate disappointment in authority figures are the same capacity, deployed in two directions.

She will, on the evidence, never resolve this relationship. The Sheriff is unlikely to provide the apology that would allow integration, and the subject is unlikely to stop needing it. The mature adaptation is not resolution but containment: she has learned to schedule the contact, brace for the contact, and recover from the contact.

### 7.5 Romantic Architecture: The Hot-Then-Exit Pattern

Across the documented partner list — Zapper, Daniel "Danny" Ridge, Wyatt Wingfoot, John Jameson (marriage, annulment), Hercules, Juggernaut, Starfox, Jack of Hearts, and several less-substantiated entries — a single architecture recurs with near-perfect fidelity:

1. **Selection criteria.** Partners are filtered, consciously or not, on at least one of two axes: (a) **physical parity or superiority** — they can take a punch, they will not break under She-Hulk's strength, the vulnerability differential that frightens her is neutralized; or (b) **emotional unavailability that mirrors the father** — Wingfoot's stoic distance, Jameson's compartmentalized military bearing, Juggernaut's character armor, Hercules's mythic narcissism. She does not select for emotional availability. When she briefly does (Jack of Hearts, in the Rowell era, with significant therapy behind her), it reads as developmentally novel.

2. **Initial phase: high-velocity intimacy.** She enters fast, with high sexual engagement, high verbal disclosure, high social integration of the partner into her milieu. This phase looks anxious-preoccupied to an outside observer and is genuinely felt as connection by the subject.

3. **The threshold moment.** Somewhere between weeks and months — earlier with weaker partners, later with stronger — the relationship asks for something the subject experiences as a demand for true dependency. The marker varies (a key offered, a child mentioned, an "I need you" said without hedge), but the response is patterned.

4. **The exit.** Mechanisms in descending order of frequency: relocation (case, Avengers business, off-world); partner-side disqualification she catalyzes (picks the fight that lets him leave); precipitating event she does not prevent (Starfox departure she could have legally fought harder; Jameson annulment she did not litigate); transformation refusal or insistence in a context that wrong-foots the partner. The exit is rarely framed by her as an exit. It is framed as circumstance.

5. **Post-mortem.** She processes the ending intellectually, often generously to the former partner, sometimes with real grief — and then forms a new attachment within a window that is, on the evidence, suspiciously short. The new partner usually shares structural features with the previous one.

The Starfox episode is the file's hardest data point on this architecture. The revelation that her sexual choices may have been chemically influenced struck at the precise nerve her whole adult adaptation is built around: *can I trust that I am the one choosing to be seen and chosen, or am I being managed?* Her processing — legal action, public framing, integration of the violation into her professional identity — is functional and characteristic, but the wound itself remains live and is, per §3, one of the operational pressure points.

### 7.6 Friendship: The Domain of Genuine Security

If romance is where the wound expresses itself, friendship is where the subject is closest to securely attached. The friendships of record — Louise Mason (Blonde Phantom), Patsy Walker (Hellcat), Janet Van Dyne intermittently, the GLK&H paralegal and associate cohort, certain Avengers women — exhibit features absent from her romantic life:

- **Durability across decades.** She keeps friends. The maintenance is asymmetric (she initiates more than she receives in some cases, less in others), but the bonds outlast partners by orders of magnitude.
- **Tolerated dependency.** She will ask Patsy for emotional help. She will let Louise scold her. She will accept practical care from women friends that she will not accept from male partners.
- **Tolerated visibility.** With trusted women friends she is seen in both forms, at low function, without makeup or wit — the only context outside of Bruce where she permits herself to be unperformed.
- **Mentor-capacity activation.** Younger heroes and junior associates draw out a reliably generous, attentive, take-them-seriously stance. She is good at being needed in this register because it does not threaten her with being depended on in the way romance does — the mentor role has built-in distance.

The reason the friendship domain works is structural: friendships do not require the specific kind of exclusive, dependency-tolerating intimacy that activates the maternal-loss complex. They permit closeness without demanding the threshold-crossing that triggers exit. She has, in effect, routed most of her real attachment needs through her friendships and asked her romantic life to handle desire, performance, and being-chosen — the parts she can tolerate.

### 7.7 Distrust, Betrayal, Repair

**How she distrusts.** Slowly, and with prejudice in favor of giving people second chances longer than is wise. Her default model is generous (the worldview: monsters are mostly people whose context we don't know), and her professional training reinforces evidentiary patience. When distrust does crystallize, however, it is procedural rather than affective: she builds a case, documents the pattern, and then acts with cold thoroughness. There is no middle gear between "trying to understand them" and "filing the motion."

**How she registers betrayal.** Two-stage. The acute stage is somatic — there is a tell, observable across decades: a stillness that arrives before any verbal response, a fractional delay in transformation, a face that goes professionally neutral. The metabolizing stage is verbal and lawyerly — she will, within hours, have a frame for the betrayal that organizes it, ranks it against precedent, and identifies the operative remedy. She is significantly more dangerous in the second stage than the first.

**What betrayal costs the betrayer.** Removal from the inner ring is near-permanent and rarely renegotiated. She maintains civility with people who have betrayed her at low cost to herself, which can read as forgiveness from outside but is actually a more permanent verdict than open hostility would be. She has stopped working on the relationship. The Sheriff is the only person who has betrayed her badly enough to lose her trust and continued to occupy a load-bearing position in her psyche — and he occupies it precisely because the original attachment was never securely formed and therefore was never withdrawable in the way later attachments are.

**How she repairs.** When the rupture is hers — and she will admit, with unusual readiness for a litigator, when it is — she repairs in concrete acts: showing up, doing the work, taking the case, taking the call. She does not over-apologize; she does not under-apologize. She has a functional shame response that does not collapse into self-attack. When the rupture is the other party's, she repairs only if they meet her at the door with both acknowledgment and changed behavior. She will not do the repair work for them; the lawyer in her knows what insufficient remedy looks like.

The post-Civil War II rebuilding period is the file's clearest evidence of repair capacity at scale. She did the work, on-page, in therapy, in graduated exposure, in halting reconstruction of professional and social ties. She did not pretend the rupture had not happened, and she did not let it become her permanent identity. This is the single strongest piece of evidence for her long-term relational prognosis: she is capable of the work, and she will do it.

### 7.8 The Template, Stated Plainly

The relational template repeated across every relationship in the file, in one paragraph:

*Approach the other person with high warmth and high competence. Establish quickly that you are visible, desirable, and useful. Read their response carefully for the specific kind of seeing you did not get from your father. If they offer it, lean in fast; if they cannot, find someone else who might. When the relationship reaches the threshold at which they would need to depend on you, or you on them, in a way that would activate the unmetabolized loss of your mother and the unhealed verdict of your father, exit — by moving, by working, by transforming, by picking the fight that lets them go. Maintain the friendship if possible. Tell yourself it was circumstance. Form the next attachment within the window that prevents the prior loss from settling in. Keep the cousin close, because he is the only one who ever passed the test. When he is killed, fall apart for the duration required, then do the therapy, then rebuild — because the alternative is to become what he became, and you have spent your entire adult life proving that the gamma did not have to be a curse.*

### 7.9 Operational Implications for the File

- **Recruitment / alliance:** She bonds reliably through shared work of consequence, particularly work that touches her vocational identity. Do not attempt friendship-first; attempt collaboration-first.
- **Coercion via attachment:** Threats to her friend-network (Patsy, Louise, the GLK&H circle) will produce stronger response than threats to romantic partners. Threats invoking Bruce will produce disproportionate response and should be considered destabilizing.
- **Manipulation resistance:** High, except along the precise axis of being-seen-accurately. Flattery rolls off; genuine accurate observation of her interior lands. The latter is the vector both for real connection and for exploitation, and she knows this — which is why her tolerance for people who deploy it insincerely is near zero.
- **Long-horizon prognosis:** The trajectory across forty years is toward integration, not regression. Each crisis has been metabolized more thoroughly than the last. If she sustains the current partnership and the current practice through another decade, the dismissive-avoidant baseline may shift toward earned-secure. This would be the rarest and most significant developmental outcome in her cohort.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## SECTION 6 — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

A defensive architecture is a load-bearing structure: take a beam out and you find out what was holding the roof up. Walters's structure has been stress-tested more rigorously than most subjects in the file room — three near-deaths, a flatline, the loss of her gamma-mirror, a documented consent violation, a chronic paternal wound, and the daily peculiar burden of literally choosing which body to inhabit. The defenses below are what kept her standing. They are ranked from most primitive to most mature, with operational behavior, observable tells, era-specific intensification, and failure modes specified.

---

### 6.1 PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Pre-Oedipal Register)

#### 6.1.1 Splitting (Self-Schema Bifurcation)

The foundational primitive defense, and the one that organizes the entire personality. The two-body presentation is the cleanest externalized splitting in the published superhuman record. Critically — and this is the diagnostic discriminator from a Kernbergian borderline structure — **she does not split the object world**; she splits the SELF. Others are perceived in full color, with ambivalence intact (her father is hated AND longed for, Bruce is idealized AND feared, Hercules is admired AND found ridiculous). The splitting falls entirely along the seam of her own self-representation.

*Operational behavior:*
- Verbal habit (consistent across Lee, Byrne, Slott, Tamaki) of speaking about "Jennifer" and "She-Hulk" in third-person register when describing how each "feels" about a situation, even though there is unified memory and agency.
- Wardrobe partitioning: the human-form closet trends toward conservative tailoring, muted palette, structural shoulders, professional armor. The transformed-form wardrobe is brighter, more revealing, more playful. Two complete sartorial dialects for one person.
- Photographic record: in candid images of herself as Jennifer she is more often half-turned, looking away, or behind something (a podium, a stack of files). In transformed-form images she faces camera, weight forward, hand on hip.
- Self-deprecating jokes about the human form ("the boring me," "Jen-the-disappointment") that read as comedy but are diagnostic schema disclosures.

*Failure mode:* When external circumstance pins her to the human form (the Slott jury-trial arc), the unintegrated split surfaces as dysphoric humiliation — she is being made to inhabit the schema she has spent years occluding. The behavior in those scenes (shoulders rounded, voice quieter, eye contact reduced) is not performance; it is the underlying self-state breaking through unmediated.

*Long arc:* Tamaki's run forces the integration that decades of avoidance had postponed. The post-CWII Hulk-outs are precisely the splitting structure failing: the previously stable "good me / unseen me" binary collapses, and what comes through is a third state — grey, monstrous, ego-dystonic — that she cannot assign to either pole. Recovery requires building, for the first time, a continuous self-representation that survives the body-change. She is doing that work; it is not finished.

#### 6.1.2 Somatization / Body-as-Defense

Closely related to splitting but distinct: she has used the BODY itself as a defensive structure, externalizing internal states onto physical form. Pre-trauma, anger did not need to be psychologically metabolized because it could be transformed into mass and discharged through behavior. Sadness did not need to be sat with because the gamma form did not feel it as acutely. The body did the affect work the mind did not have to do.

This is why the Tamaki-era inability to transform is so catastrophic: the defense isn't slow, it is GONE, and thirty years of unprocessed affect is now in the room with her, with no shock absorber.

#### 6.1.3 Acting-Out (Sexual and Behavioral)

Present, episodic, mid-2000s peak. The Slott-era "party girl" public profile, the rapid serial romantic engagements (Wingfoot, Jameson, Hercules, Juggernaut, Starfox in close sequence), the bar fights, the drinking. The behavior pattern is recognizable: when affect threatens to surface, she externalizes it into action — sexual, social, physical — that consumes the affective energy without requiring it to be experienced as itself.

*Discriminator from characterological promiscuity:* the acting-out is **state-dependent and stress-correlated**, not baseline. In stable periods (early Byrne, Soule middle, current Rowell) the behavior recedes. She is not running a libidinal economy of conquest; she is discharging.

---

### 6.2 NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Mid-Level)

#### 6.2.1 Intellectualization

The law is the cathedral of this defense. When affect threatens, she retreats to procedure, statute, case-citation, doctrinal frame. The Civil War registration position is the textbook example: faced with the affective horror of friends declaring civil war on each other, she defaults to the institutional/legal analysis ("the law is the law, registration is constitutional, my role is to prosecute") and rides the frame past the feeling. The Starfox processing is the same defense in adaptive mode: she metabolizes a sexual violation by filing suit.

*Operational tells:*
- Latinate vocabulary spikes under emotional pressure (observe the syntactic shift in any scene where she is being asked about Bruce: clauses lengthen, abstract nouns proliferate).
- The "I'd like to brief that before I answer" reflex in personal conversation, played for laughs by every writer who has touched her but consistent enough across runs to be a real verbal tic.
- Tendency to convert relational disputes into negotiations with terms ("if you do X by Tuesday, I will do Y").

*Failure mode:* When the legal frame cannot reach the injury — Bruce's death is not a legal problem, Banner cannot be sued back to life — the defense collapses and there is nothing immediately behind it. The Tamaki isolation period is partly what happens when intellectualization runs out of cases to work.

#### 6.2.2 Reaction Formation (Paternal Axis)
