Durability sufficient to survive orbital reentry, sustained heavy-weapons fire, and the Thanos engagement that flatlined her. Accelerated healing measured in minutes-to-hours for tissue insults that would kill a baseline human in seconds. None of this is the headline asset. The headline asset is what is **preserved** through the transformation.

**Cognitive preservation under transformation.** Unlike the cousin (Banner, B.), the subject suffers no IQ decrement, no language degradation, no executive-function loss, no dissociative amnesia between forms. She is the same mind in two chassis. This is, in the literature of gamma-affected individuals, statistically aberrant and functionally unique. The operational implication: she is the only known gamma-mutate who can practice law, argue a brief, run a negotiation, or perform surgical-grade tactical reasoning **while** carrying the strength tier of a planetary-defense asset. No one else in her cohort combines those two registers in a single body.

**The baseline body.** Even in human form, the subject post-incident retains accelerated healing, elevated baseline strength, fatigue resistance, and a metabolism that defeats most intoxicants and most poisons. The "vulnerable" form is, by civilian standards, still exceptional. Subject undervalues this; observers should not.

**Dual-form code-switching capacity.** The ability to choose form by context is itself a capability. She can clear a hostile room without bringing the green form into a courtroom; she can de-escalate a domestic situation in human scale and then engage the underlying combatant at her own scale; she can disappear into a crowd or fill a doorway. Most operators have one body. She has two and the executive function to deploy each appropriately.

**Voluntary control (post-recovery).** After the Tamaki-era decompensation and the therapy work, voluntary transformation has been restored — with the caveat that it now requires conscious affect-regulation rather than ambient ease. This is, paradoxically, a more **robust** capability than the pre-trauma version: she now knows how she does it.

---

### 9.2 COGNITIVE ASSETS

**Verbal intelligence (high, possibly 99th percentile).** Demonstrated across forty years of dialogue, briefs, cross-examinations, fourth-wall asides, and improvised banter under combat load. Lexical access is fast, syntactically complex, and stylistically range-controlled — she can speak court-formal, peer-collegial, street-vernacular, and superhuman-domain shorthand without code-switch latency.

**Working memory.** Holds multiple case theories, opposing counsel's argument tree, the judge's prior rulings, the client's instructions, and the relevant statutory matrix simultaneously. This is observable in any sustained Slott-era courtroom sequence; it also shows up in combat as the capacity to track multiple opponents and a civilian-evacuation problem in the same engagement.

**Common-law / analogical reasoning.** Her native mode. She thinks in cases, precedents, fact-patterns. This is a particularly **transferable** cognitive style: it works in court, in negotiation, in tactical planning, in interpersonal diagnosis. She pattern-matches across domains faster than most domain-specialists pattern-match within their own.

**Adversarial cognition under load.** Trained and temperamental. She gets sharper under cross-examination, not duller. Pressure compresses her thinking into clarity rather than dispersing it into noise. Operationally: the worse the situation, the better her output, up to the threshold where trauma response takes over (a much higher threshold than for most).

**Meta-cognition.** She knows how she thinks. The "courtroom in the head" — the running self-cross-examination — is a liability when it becomes rumination, but it is an asset when it functions as quality control on her own reasoning. She catches her own errors. She updates.

**Humor as cognitive instrument.** Not decoration. Her wit is a working tool — for de-escalation, for sense-making under threat, for building rapport across status gaps, for puncturing pretension (including her own), and for the fourth-wall-aware authorial distance that has historically allowed her to survive being looked at. A subject who can make a joke about her own situation has, by the act of making it, established that some part of her is standing outside the situation. That standing-outside is a survival asset.

---

### 9.3 VOCATIONAL ASSETS

**The license.** Member of the bar in good standing, multiple jurisdictions inferable, with a documented sub-specialty in superhuman law that is effectively a niche of one for long stretches. This is not a credential; it is a **load-bearing identity structure**. When affect threatens to overwhelm, she has somewhere to go that is real, useful, and validated by an external institution. Most people do not have an epistemology they can retreat into; she does.

**Domain expertise — superhuman law.** Possibly the deepest expert in the field. Knows the registration statutes, the precedent on powered testimony, the evidentiary rules for telepathic evidence, the immigration questions for extraterrestrials, the property law of artifacts, the criminal liability frameworks for shape-shifters, the corporate structures of hero-licensing. This is institutional knowledge that cannot be reproduced quickly by any competitor.

**GLK&H and successor practice infrastructure.** Documented track record at Goodman, Lieber, Kurtzberg & Holliway and at her own subsequent practice arrangements. Reputation among the superhuman client base is high; she gets the calls. Referral network is mature.

**Courtroom presence.** In either form. The Slott-era humiliation of being forced to appear as Jennifer was psychologically painful precisely because she was, even then, **effective in that form**. Juries listen to her. Judges respect her even when annoyed. Opposing counsel underestimate the human-form Walters at predictable cost.

**Negotiation capacity.** Underdocumented in the canon but inferable from outcomes: she settles cases, brokers truces between powered factions, brings the Avengers and the FF and street-level operators to the same table when called. The Civil War positioning, whatever one thinks of it, demonstrated her willingness to be the person in the room where the institution is being argued with rather than walked out on.

---

### 9.4 SOCIAL & RELATIONAL ASSETS

**Friend-keeper across decades.** Patsy Walker (Hellcat) — the longest-running female friendship in the file, mutually trauma-aware, mutually irreverent, durable through multiple deaths and resurrections on both sides. Louise Mason (the Blonde Phantom) — mentor-friendship across generational lines. The GLK&H bullpen — Pug, Augustus Pugliese, the paralegals, the support staff, treated with documented respect over years. Janet Van Dyne, on and off. Various Avengers (Carol Danvers especially) who answer her calls.

The pattern: **friendships outlast romances by a factor of approximately ten**. The relational architecture that fails her in pair-bonding succeeds her in chosen-family. This is not a deficit to be corrected; it is an asset to be recognized. Her primary attachment system runs on friendship, not romance, and the friendship system is healthy.

**Peer-group access at the highest tier.** She is in the room with the Avengers, the Future Foundation, the Defenders-adjacent networks, the bar associations, the Illuminati-adjacent legal apparatus. When she calls, people pick up. This is social capital accumulated through decades of competent collaborative behavior.

**Mentor capacity, demonstrated.** Junior associates, younger heroes (canonically she has taken time with several), the next-generation gamma figures when they appear. She does not hoard authority; she trains.

**Cross-status fluency.** She moves between superhuman gala and public defender's office, between Latverian state dinner and dive bar, between Asgardian feast and Brooklyn deposition, without affect mismatch. The range is real and rare.

---

### 9.5 PSYCHOLOGICAL ASSETS

**Demonstrated capacity to do the work.** This is the single most important entry in the entire ledger. The post-Civil War II decompensation could have been terminal; in many comparable cases of trauma-stacking (combat veteran, mass-casualty survivor, primary loss of attachment figure to friendly-fire), the trajectory is chronic disability or worse. She entered therapy on-page, stayed in it, used it, and rebuilt function. **A subject who has proven she can recover from a full breakdown is, all else equal, more reliable than a subject who has never been tested.**

**Integrated humor.** Not deflection — integration. Her wit acknowledges the painful thing while continuing to operate around it. This is a mature defense in the Vaillant sense and a stable feature across all eras.

**Sublimation as a primary defense.** Aggression channeled into combat against actual aggressors; exhibitionism channeled into courtroom performance and heroic visibility; mother-loss channeled into protective vocation. The energies that would otherwise leak into pathology have functional channels.

**Accountability instinct.** She holds herself responsible. Civil War, whatever one's politics, was a stand taken in public with her name on it; the Starfox prosecution was an injury named and litigated rather than buried; the post-Bruce period included explicit on-page recognition that her own rage was hers, not the form's. Subjects who can say "that was me" are more workable than subjects who cannot.

**Capacity for shame, in the healthy register.** She is capable of being embarrassed, of regretting, of apologizing — and of doing so without collapsing. This is the prosocial emotion that narcissistic-spectrum subjects lack; its presence is a strong prognostic marker.

**Empathic range.** She empathizes with clients across the moral spectrum, with opposing parties, with monsters (because most monsters are people whose context is missing), with her cousin even when he is the threat. This is not naïveté; it is a trained-and-temperamental ability to model other minds, which is also a tactical asset.

**Stable narrative identity.** Across forty years, she has a coherent story about who she is. The story has been revised — significantly, after Civil War II — but it remains coherent. She is not a person with identity diffusion. Compare again: Banner, whose narrative coherence is the thing his condition specifically attacks.

---

### 9.6 MORAL & WORLDVIEW ASSETS

**A working operational code.** The law is real. Institutions are imperfect but improvable from inside. Power must be accountable, including her own. Humor is a moral act. Family is what you make. These are not slogans; they are the actual predictive priors of her decision-making, and they have been stable across forty years and multiple writers' attempts to bend her.

**Prosocial default.** When uncertain, she defaults to protect-the-vulnerable. This is observable in arc after arc.

**Rule-following without rule-worship.** She respects process while remaining willing to argue with judges, gods, the Sheriff, the President. She is not a Lawful Stupid figure; she is a Lawful figure with conscience-driven exceptions, which is the operationally useful version.

**No documented cruelty.** Across four decades of stress, conflict, and provocation, the file contains no instance of cruelty as such. Anger, yes. Force, yes. Retribution, yes. Cruelty for its own sake, no. This is rarer in the cohort than is generally acknowledged.

---

### 9.7 RESOURCE ASSETS

**Income.** Specialized practice at her level, in her market, generates substantial professional income. She is not financially vulnerable.

**Housing/geographic flexibility.** Has lived and practiced in Los Angeles, New York, and intermediate locations; can relocate as situation requires.

**Network-as-resource.** The Avengers infrastructure, the FF infrastructure, the bar association, the GLK&H alumni network, and the broader superhuman community function as a force-multiplier on her individual capabilities. She can call in favors at scale.

**Information access.** Through her practice, she has visibility into the legal status, capabilities, and entanglements of most of the major powered actors in her hemisphere. She is one of the most **informed** subjects in her cohort, simply by virtue of her client list.

---

### 9.8 RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHY THE STRENGTHS HOLD

Strengths can be inventoried by anyone; what makes them durable is harder to map. The following are the structural reasons this subject's asset ledger does not collapse under stress the way comparable ledgers do.

**Redundancy across domains.** Her identity is not load-bearing on any single pillar. If the gamma form is taken (as in the FF stripping arc), she has the practice. If the practice is suspended, she has the heroic community. If the heroic community fails her (as post-CWII), she has the friendships. If the friendships are unreachable, she has the work of articulation itself. The failure of one pillar does not bring the structure down.

**The cousin as cautionary referent.** She has watched, in close family detail, what happens when the work is not done. Banner is her permanent reminder of the alternative trajectory. This is a powerful and unusual resilience asset: a vivid, loved, intimate negative example.

**Form as choice.** After the early involuntary period, the transformation became chosen. The experience of having chosen one's own body — repeatedly, against external pressure to revert — generates a durable sense of agency that survives most insults to it.

**The Bruce internalization.** Even after his death, the introject of the kind cousin remains. She carries a model of being-seen-with-kindness that her father failed to provide and her mother died before completing. The introject is good-enough for the regulatory function and is permanent.

**Trauma-tested.** She has been through the worst version of her own collapse and come out the other side. The next collapse, when it comes, will be approached by a self that has the memory of having survived the previous one.

**Therapy-literate.** She has done the work, on-page, without irony, and the language and frame of clinical recovery are now part of her toolkit. She can name her own panic attacks. She can describe her own avoidance. This is a capability the vast majority of comparable subjects lack.

**Vocational ground.** When everything else is in motion, the law stays still. Statutes do not move because she is having a bad day. The objectivity of the external frame is, for a subject whose internal frame is contested, a profound stabilizer.

**Humor as immune system.** A subject who can still make a joke is a subject whose central nervous system is still online. Her humor function has survived every era; its persistence is itself a diagnostic of underlying health.

---

### 9.9 OPERATIONAL SUMMARY

The subject's asset profile is **broad, deep, redundant, and battle-tested**. She is not the strongest gamma-mutate, not the most decorated Avenger, not the most prominent attorney. She is something rarer: an integrated operator whose capabilities in two normally non-overlapping domains (Class-100 physical engagement and elite legal practice) are housed in a single continuously-conscious self with a working moral code, a durable friendship network, a demonstrated recovery trajectory from severe trauma, and a sense of humor that has outlasted everyone who tried to take it from her.

The benevolent reading of this file is straightforward: **the work she has done on herself is the asset, and everything else is a multiplier on it.** The strengths catalogued above are not gifts. They are, with the partial exception of the gamma physiology, **earned positions** — held against pressure, lost and recovered, and held again.

A surveillance apparatus building a file on her in order to predict her would conclude: she is unusually predictable in the prosocial direction, unusually resilient under load, and unusually likely to do the right and difficult thing when it is offered to her in terms her articulation-mastery can metabolize. She is, in operational terms, **trustworthy at scale** — which is, in this cohort, the rarest asset of all.

— *UATU, observing.*


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## Section 6 — FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

The subject does not fail loudly at first. This is the central operational fact and the reason her collapses have historically caught her colleagues — and herself — by surprise. Her baseline functioning is so high, her wit so reflexive, her vocational output so consistent, that the early phases of decompensation are misread as ordinary fatigue, ordinary irritability, ordinary "Jen having a week." She has spent her entire adult life constructing a presentation that looks load-bearing precisely so that no one will check whether it is. The result is a subject whose breakdowns, when they come, present at Stage 3 or 4 of an escalation ladder that nobody around her — and often she herself — was tracking from Stage 1.

What follows is the longitudinal pattern, derived from forty-plus years of observable behavior under stress, mapped to the conditions that reliably produce it.

---

### 6.1 The Escalation Ladder

**Stage 0 — Baseline-plus (the warning state nobody recognizes as a warning).**
The earliest detectable signal is *increased output*. She files more motions. She accepts more cases. She returns emails faster, at odder hours. Her humor sharpens — wittier, more pointed, with a faintly cruel edge that is absent at true baseline. She becomes a marginally better lawyer and a marginally less generous person, and because the first effect is more visible than the second, it reads as competence rather than compensation. Social calendar tightens around utility contacts (peers, colleagues, professional events); personal contacts (Louise Mason, Patsy Walker) get shorter, more transactional calls. Workouts intensify. Sleep contracts by 60-90 minutes a night without subjective complaint. This is the phase where the courtroom-in-the-head goes from background hum to constant argument; if a surveillance file had her phone, the late-night searches would shift from recipes and case law to case law only.

**Stage 1 — Hypercompetence as defense.**
She begins to *prefer* the green form for ordinary tasks. Grocery runs, court appearances that don't require it, casual social events — she goes She-Hulk by default. Coworkers register this as "Jen's mood." It is the first observable sign that the human-form schema is being avoided. Sexual self-presentation rises: more flirtation, more visible self-display, more deployment of the body she controls in the form she controls. Drinking, if she is in a period where she drinks, becomes nightly rather than social. She tells nobody anything is wrong because nothing, from inside, *is* wrong yet; she is doing all the things she does when she is fine, only more.

**Stage 2 — Affective leakage.**
The first cracks present as irritability misaligned with stimulus. A clerk's small error produces a disproportionate response, immediately walked back, apologized for, brooded on. She starts running geographic and relational distance plays: she will move (apartments, cities — across her published life she has changed primary residence repeatedly under stress), end a relationship she was three weeks ago describing as promising, take an out-of-town case to put physical distance between herself and a triggering proximity. The exits are always rationalized in the language of opportunity, never of avoidance, and the rationalizations are good — she is a *lawyer* — but the pattern is legible across decades: the closer something gets to the maternal-loss/paternal-rejection complex, the further she physically goes. Sexual acting-out intensifies in this phase and acquires a quality of grim performance; the partners get less considered, the encounters less integrated into the rest of her life.

**Stage 3 — Procedural fortification.**
This is the phase the Civil War posture exemplifies. When affect threatens to overwhelm, she retreats hard into the law as a fixed object. Positions become more rigid; nuance, normally her strong suit, contracts. She begins to argue from authority rather than from analysis. She will prosecute someone she likes, defend a position she has private doubts about, and sustain the procedural frame past the point where her better judgment would normally have intervened, because the frame is doing structural work that has nothing to do with the case. Colleagues who know her well notice that she stops asking questions she would normally ask. The intellectualization is total and articulate and almost impossible to argue with from outside. Sleep is now significantly disrupted; she is working in the small hours, and the work is good, and the work is also the wall.

**Stage 4 — Somatic intrusion.**
The body begins to refuse to follow the script. Transformations become *off-schedule* — either failing to come when called, or arriving uninvited. Post-CWII this presented as the gray-flavored Hulk-out: rage-driven, frightening to herself, ego-dystonic. Earlier in her career it presented as involuntary transformation under stress. The common feature is the loss of the bodily agency she has organized her entire identity around. Panic episodes appear, sometimes in objectively safe contexts (her own apartment, a familiar courtroom). Hyperarousal is now visible to anyone paying attention: startle response, scanning behavior, a particular flinch at sudden physical proximity from behind. She begins to avoid the transformation in either direction — afraid to Hulk out because of what arrives, afraid to be Jennifer because of the small-girl schema waiting there. The two-body solution that organized her life stops working.

**Stage 5 — Collapse.**
Functional withdrawal. She does not show up. The phone is off. The apartment is fortified by routine — Tamaki's run documents this with clinical fidelity: micromanaged days, narrow allowed activities, the deliberate construction of a life so small no affect can fit inside it. She will isolate from precisely the people most equipped to help her, because being seen in this state is intolerable to a subject whose core wound is around being seen incorrectly. The wit goes silent. This is the loudest signal — when Jennifer Walters is not making a joke, the system is in failure. She becomes capable, in this phase, of destructive outbursts that she experiences afterward with profound shame, and the shame loops back into further isolation.

**Stage 6 — Rebuild.**
Recovery, when it comes, is slow and structured and explicit. Therapy on-page (Tamaki's run makes this canonical). Deliberate, graded exposure to the transformation. Reconstruction of community starting with one or two trusted persons (Patsy Walker has played this role; Jack of Hearts has played a version of it). Return to practice in small, controlled increments. The rebuild is real and it works — but it is permanent work now, not a recovery to a prior baseline. The pre-CWII relationship to the green form is gone; what replaces it is more integrated, more conscious, and more effortful.

---

### 6.2 Decompensation Signatures by Domain

**Verbal/cognitive.** The first thing to watch is her sentences. At baseline she speaks in clean, complete, often funny constructions with a courtroom rhythm — claim, evidence, qualification, landing. Under early decompensation the qualifications drop out; she becomes more declarative, more clipped. Under deeper decompensation the humor flattens — still present, but mechanical, deployed reflexively without the warmth that normally accompanies it. At Stage 5 she goes quiet, and when she speaks the syntax is short and the affect is absent. A surveillance log of her speech alone would be a reliable barometer.

**Somatic tells.** Jaw tension is the persistent one — visible in the human form, present but masked in the green. A specific habit of pressing the heel of her hand against her sternum, briefly, when something lands hard; almost subliminal, easy to miss, present across runs. Hand-to-back-of-neck when she is being asked something she does not want to answer. In the green form, a tendency to fold her arms across her chest — a posture that does not read as defensive on a body that size, which is exactly why she uses it. Under acute stress she will, in either form, place her palms flat on a surface — table, desk, wall — and look at her own hands. It is a grounding gesture she does not appear to know she is performing.

**Sleep.** Contraction is the early signal; fragmentation is the middle signal; nightmares with somatic content (the GSW, the transfusion, Bruce) are the late signal. Post-CWII, sleep onset itself becomes a feared event. She will work to exhaustion to avoid the threshold.

**Relational.** Cancellations rise. Replies get shorter. She begins to triage human contact by anticipated emotional demand, accepting the low-demand contacts (work, colleagues, casual peers) and shedding the high-demand ones (close friends, family, anyone who might ask the question). Romantic partners are either pulled closer in a brief, intense pull or pushed out entirely; the middle distance she normally sustains becomes unavailable.

**Vocational.** Output rises before it falls. The fall, when it comes, is sudden — she does not taper, she stops. Missed filings are essentially never seen at baseline; their appearance is a Stage 4-5 marker and would be the signal a professional observer would weight most heavily.

**Substance.** Alcohol use, when present, scales with stage. The mid-2000s pattern shows the full curve: social drinking → nightly drinking → drinking-to-permit-behavior → drinking-to-not-feel. Gamma metabolism prevents the physiological dependence that would otherwise complicate the picture, which is itself a problem: there is no hangover-floor to force a pause. The behavioral pattern can sustain indefinitely without the biological brake other subjects experience.

---

### 6.3 The Conditions That Produce It

The decompensation is not random. It is reliably triggered by a small, specific set of inputs, alone or in combination:

**The father, in any form.** Direct contact with William Walters, news of him, a court appearance in his jurisdiction, a father-figure transference onto a judge or senior partner, even a procedural reminder of LA County. The complex is unmetabolized; any live wire to it produces disproportionate affect, which she immediately defends against, beginning the ladder.

**Bruce, in any form.** Invocation, anniversary, a gamma case that touches the family physiology, an encounter with someone who knew him. The grief is integrated but not closed; it is a load the system carries continuously, and additional weight on that vector breaks things faster than weight on any other.

**Forced form-mismatch.** Being required to appear as Jennifer when the situation demands She-Hulk authority (the Slott courtroom scenes), or as She-Hulk when she has chosen Jennifer. The injury is specifically to her bodily agency — to her right to choose which body meets which world — and it activates the deepest drive in the personality, which is the right to be seen on her own terms.

**Sexual agency violations or their echoes.** The Starfox precedent established that this category of injury bypasses her normal defenses and goes straight to the procedural-fortification response. She will pursue these adversarially and competently and will also, privately, decompensate around them. The two are not in tension; the pursuit is part of the decompensation pattern, not separate from it.

**Threats to vocational standing.** Her bar license, her firm position, her standing among superhuman counsel — these are load-bearing for the entire self-concept. A threat here produces immediate Stage 3 fortification and, if sustained, accelerates through the ladder.

**Being looked at without being seen.** The precise injury her architecture is built to prevent. Public sexualization without recognition of personhood; admiration of She-Hulk that erases Jennifer; admiration of Jennifer that condescends to the form she has chosen. This is the slow-acting trigger — a single instance does little; sustained exposure (a press cycle, a public scandal, a period of being a tabloid object) produces a months-long decompensation.

**Survivor situations.** Any context in which she lives and someone else dies, particularly when the dying happens at allied hands or when she experienced clinical death herself. The CWII pattern is the template. She does not metabolize survivor guilt quickly and does not have a religious or philosophical frame that absorbs it; the law does not have a doctrine for *why I lived*, and the absence of doctrine is felt as absence of ground.

**Compound triggers.** The catastrophic decompensations occur when two or more of these vectors load simultaneously. CWII was: near-death + survivor guilt + Bruce-loss + form-failure, all inside a window of weeks. The system has redundancies for any one input. It does not have redundancies for three.

---

### 6.4 What Collapse Looks Like, Specifically

A fully decompensated Jennifer Walters is not a rampaging figure. She is, instead, a woman who has made her world very small. The apartment is clean in a way it is not normally clean — the clean of someone with too much time and too much need for control over surfaces. The phone is face-down. The calendar has been emptied of anything optional and most things that aren't. Meals are functional and repetitive. She is working, but on solo tasks that do not require her to speak to anyone — research, drafting, the parts of practice that can be done alone in a chair at 3 a.m. She has not transformed in days or weeks, and the question of whether she can is one she is actively avoiding asking herself. When she does transform, it is sudden, frightening, and brief, and she will not speak about it afterward.

The people who would normally hear from her do not. When they reach her, she is fine; she is just busy; she will call next week. She will not call next week. If they show up at the door she will let them in and she will be funny, and the funny will be a fraction of a beat off, and the better friends among them will recognize this and stay, and she will, eventually, after some hours, tell one of them something true. This is the inflection point. If a friend is in the room when she tells the true thing, she begins climbing back. If no one is, she does not.

The destructive episodes, when they occur, are short and contained and followed by extended shame. She does not break things in public. She breaks things alone, and then she repairs or replaces them, and then she sits with what she has done, and the sitting is worse than the breaking.

The worst version — the version the file must contemplate even though it has not yet occurred on-page — would involve a compound trigger striking during a period when she is already isolated from the people who could intervene. In that scenario the green form's escalation, untempered by the cousin's tragic example which she has always held as a *do-not-become*, becomes the controlling risk. She is one of the strongest beings on the planet. She has, to date and to her credit, never been the worst version of what that could mean. The reason she has not is not luck; it is the work, the friendships, and the vocation. Any sustained removal of those three would change the risk profile materially.

---

### 6.5 Operational Summary

Subject fails *quietly, competently, and late*. The early phases of her decompensation look like excellence and must be read against her own baseline, not against an external standard. The most reliable indicators are: contraction of the qualifying clause in her speech, drop-off in unprompted humor, default-to-green for tasks that do not require it, cancellation of high-intimacy contacts while maintaining low-intimacy ones, and sleep contraction without subjective complaint. The most catastrophic triggers are compound: any two of (father, Bruce, form-mismatch, sexual violation, vocational threat, survivor situation) striking inside a narrow window. The recovery pattern is robust when activated but requires external scaffolding — therapy, at least one trusted person in physical proximity, and a return to vocational ground — and does not activate spontaneously from full Stage 5 isolation. The single most protective intervention, across her entire published life, has been the presence of a person who can be in the room when she tells the true thing. Resource allocation should reflect this.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WALTERS, JENNIFER SUSAN
## SECTION 9 — TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

---

### 9.0 Frame of the Assessment

The subject is in her late twenties by operational reckoning, post-trauma, post-reconstitution, mid-rebuild. The trajectory question is therefore not "will she stabilize" — she has demonstrated, across the Rowell-era reconsolidation, that she can — but rather *at what level* she stabilizes, *what shape* the stabilization takes, and *which of the unresolved structural questions* she finally moves on versus continues to postpone. The file's working assumption is that Walters is now in the most psychologically generative window of her adult life: the trauma forced her to develop affect-regulation capacities she had previously outsourced to her gamma physiology, and she now possesses both the prior gifts (verbal facility, professional vocation, durable friendships, integrated humor) and the new capacities (felt knowledge of her own limits, therapeutic literacy, an intimate relationship with fear that she did not previously have). She has the tools. The question is whether she uses them on the deeper architecture or only on its symptoms.

What follows maps the realistic 1-year, 3-5-year, and 10+-year horizons; identifies the fork points where small choices produce large divergences; enumerates the open questions the file cannot yet answer; and specifies the conditions that would move her toward growth versus the conditions that would move her toward catastrophe.

---

### 9.1 Twelve-Month Horizon — The Reconsolidation Window

The next twelve months are predicted to be outwardly the most placid of the post-CWII period and inwardly the most decisive. Expected surface developments:

- **Practice rebuild to roughly 70-80% of pre-trauma capacity.** She will not return to GLK&H volume; she will instead operate a smaller, more selective practice, almost certainly out of a leased one- or two-attorney office space in Manhattan, with a paralegal she trusts and a docket weighted toward superhuman civil rights, wrongful-power-suppression suits, and the occasional high-visibility criminal defense that she takes for the principle. She will turn down work that previously she would have accepted reflexively. This is growth, not retreat.
- **Stabilization of the romantic re-partnering** at a sustained but boundaried level. The pattern to watch: she will not move in. She will keep her own apartment. She will introduce the partner to her peer group selectively. If she sustains a partnership past the eighteen-month mark — historically her exit zone — that is itself a structural change worth flagging.
- **Re-engagement with the transformation on the order of three to five times per week**, primarily in deliberately chosen, non-emergency contexts: workouts, social occasions where she wants to occupy the form, the occasional patrol. This is exposure therapy in the form of daily life. Expect at least one minor backslide — an unbidden Hulk-out under acute stress in which she frightens herself — within the first six months. Whether she pathologizes it or processes it will be the leading indicator.
- **Continued therapy at reduced frequency** (biweekly trending to monthly). Termination not recommended and, on the evidence of her own insight, not likely to be initiated by her in this window.

The deep work in this window is invisible: the gradual reintegration of the human form as an inhabitable body rather than a costume worn under duress. The single most diagnostic behavior to track is whether she chooses to spend more or fewer waking hours in human form than she did pre-trauma. Pre-CWII she ran ~10-20% human. A move toward 30-50% human would indicate she is doing the hardest piece of the work; a snap back to ≤10% would indicate she is using the green form as avoidance again.

---

### 9.2 Three-to-Five-Year Horizon — The Integration or Reversion Fork

By the three-year mark the trajectory bifurcates sharply, and the bifurcation is best described as **integration vs. reversion**.

**The integration trajectory.** The form-bifurcation collapses functionally: Jennifer and She-Hulk become not two selves but two registers of one self, the way most people have a "work voice" and a "home voice." She enters the form when situationally indicated, exits it when situationally indicated, and the choice carries no more affective weight than choosing what to wear. The romantic relationship deepens or, if it ends, ends cleanly and is followed by a non-frantic next attempt. The practice expands by hiring rather than by personal overwork. She takes on a public-facing role in the bar — superhuman law section chair, amicus author of record on a landmark case, possibly a teaching appointment at Columbia or NYU. She reopens contact with her father on her terms, on a schedule she controls, with stakes she defines. She does not reconcile with him in any deep sense — that is not available — but she stops organizing her life around the distance from him. Around year four or five, the file expects either a serious cohabitation/marriage decision or a deliberate, articulated choice not to pursue one, which would itself be a mature outcome rather than the avoidance it would have been a decade earlier.

**The reversion trajectory.** A second major trauma — and the operational tempo of her cohort makes this more likely than not within five years — re-fractures the integration. She returns to the pre-CWII pattern of living in the green form full-time, but without the easy pleasure she once took in it; the form becomes a defensive shell rather than a chosen expression. The relationship ends at the eighteen-month mark per old pattern. The practice stagnates or, worse, becomes a hiding place — long hours, procedural over-focus, declining outside-of-work life. Drinking returns at the mid-2000s level or above. She does not, in this trajectory, decompensate dramatically; she simply contracts. The Walters reversion mode is quiet, not loud. It looks like high function and feels, from the inside, like exhaustion.

**The fork point** between these is small and identifiable: it is her response to the *next* significant loss. Not the catastrophic loss — those overwhelm anyone — but the medium loss: a friend's serious injury, a case lost on appeal, the partner ending things, the father's eventual death. If she treats the medium loss as something to be metabolized in therapy and with her peer group, she stays on the integration line. If she treats it as something to be outworked, outdrunk, or out-Hulked, she crosses into reversion.

---

### 9.3 Ten-Plus-Year Horizon — The Long Arc

The long arc, if integration holds, points toward something the comics cohort rarely produces: a mature professional in her forties who has done her grief work, who occupies her body without ambivalence, who has chosen her family rather than waited for one, and whose superhuman identity is one fact among many about her rather than the defining one. The likely shape:

- **Vocational:** federal bench candidacy is not absurd to consider by year ten. She has the intellect, the bar standing, and the public profile. The obstacles are the Avengers record (some senators will treat it as disqualifying), the past relational chaos (opposition research goldmine), and her own ambivalence about whether judging would suit her temperamentally — she is an advocate by disposition, not an umpire. More likely she becomes a named partner in a boutique superhuman-rights firm, or the founding director of a superhuman legal aid clinic, or both. A book — likely a casebook, possibly a memoir she would resist writing for a decade and then write — is probable.
- **Heroic:** reduced operational tempo, increased mentor function. She will not retire; the form is too constitutive. But the pattern shifts from front-line Avenger to senior counsel, instructor, the person younger heroes call before they call a lawyer. A team-leadership role — Avengers chair, Defenders convenor — is plausible if she wants it and possible to decline if she doesn't.
- **Relational:** the open question of the file. Three plausible long-term shapes: (a) sustained partnership, possibly marriage, with someone who can hold both registers of her and who is not himself a crisis generator; (b) deliberately chosen single life with a deep peer network functioning as chosen family; (c) the old serial pattern, indefinitely, which would by year ten read not as searching but as settled avoidance. (a) and (b) are both growth outcomes; (c) is the diagnostic sign that the underlying schema was never reworked.
- **Reproductive:** the canon's oblique treatment of her gestational incompatibility leaves this genuinely unresolved. If she wants children, the path is adoption, surrogacy, or a medical-scientific resolution she has the connections to pursue. The file's reading is that she has not, as of latest data, decided whether she wants this; the question has been postponed because the prior conditions for asking it (stable partnership, stable self) were not present. They are becoming present. Expect the question to surface, painfully, in the three-to-five-year window.

---

### 9.4 The Open Questions

The file flags the following as genuinely undecided, not as predictions:

1. **The father.** Will she initiate the conversation she has avoided for twenty-plus years — the one about her mother's death, the blame, the lifetime of withholding — or will she let it be foreclosed by his death? Both are possible. The first is the growth outcome and the harder one; the second is the more probable one given the avoidance pattern, and would leave a permanent unmetabolized residue she would carry into every subsequent attachment.
2. **The cousin.** Bruce's death is metabolized but not closed. The Marvel cosmology being what it is, his return in some form is a near-certainty on a ten-year horizon. The question is whether his return finds her ready to receive him as a peer, having done her own work in his absence, or whether it short-circuits the work by restoring the mirror she lost. The first is integrative; the second is regressive in a way that would look, superficially, like healing.
3. **The form, as she ages.** She is in her late twenties now. The transformation has been her primary self-presentation for most of her adult life. As the human form ages and the gamma form, presumably, does not — or ages differently — the bifurcation will acquire a new dimension she has not yet had to face. By her forties this becomes a live question; by her fifties it becomes structural. The file cannot predict her response, only flag that no era of canon has yet tested it.
4. **The sexual-agency wound.** The Starfox episode was processed legally and articulately, but the file's assessment is that the *somatic* residue — the question of which of her past desires were truly hers — has not been fully addressed in therapy. It is the kind of injury that surfaces unpredictably, often years later, often in the context of a new intimate relationship where trust is being built. Expect it to recur as an issue. Whether she meets it with the same articulate frame or whether it produces a deeper dysregulation is open.
5. **The exhibitionistic register.** The fourth-wall-breaking, the performance-of-being-looked-at, the preemptive control of the gaze — this is a defense that has also been a genuine pleasure and a source of agency. The file does not assume she should give it up; integration may look like keeping it but no longer needing it. The open question is whether she can tell the difference.
6. **The drinking.** Currently quiescent. The biology may prevent dependency but the behavioral pattern is intact and reactivatable. No prediction; a flag.

---

### 9.5 Growth Vectors — What Would Push Her Toward Integration

In rough order of leverage:

- **Continuity of therapy past the point of feeling done.** The next phase of work — the schema-level work on the small-girl self-representation, the father transference, the maternal absence — is the work she has not yet done because the crisis work was prior. She is now positioned to do it. Whether she chooses to is the single largest variable in her long-term trajectory.
- **A sustained partnership that survives the eighteen-month threshold.** Not because partnership is the index of health, but because for *her* specifically, sustained partnership is the territory where the avoidant pattern has to be confronted rather than dodged.
- **Mentoring relationships, both directions.** Being mentored by someone older — the file flags the absence of a stable older-woman figure in her life as significant; her friendships are largely peer — and mentoring younger attorneys and heroes. The latter she already does well. The former is missing and would materially help.
- **A deliberate confrontation with the father, on her timeline.** Whatever its outcome, the act of initiating closes a loop the avoidance has held open.
- **Physical practice in the human form** — sustained, deliberate occupation of the body she has spent her life avoiding. Athletics, dance, embodiment work. The therapeutic literature is clear and her case fits the indication.
- **A creative or scholarly project in her own voice** — the casebook, the memoir, a podcast on superhuman law, anything that puts her articulation to work on her own life rather than her clients'.
- **Reduced operational tempo as an Avenger.** Counterintuitive, but the heroic register has at times functioned as a sublimation that prevents the underlying work. Doing less front-line work would force more sitting with the self.

---

### 9.6 Catastrophic Vectors — What Would Push Her Toward Collapse

Also in rough order, weighted by likelihood:

- **A second catastrophic loss in the peer circle before the first is fully metabolized.** Patsy Walker, Louise Mason, Jack of Hearts, the GLK&H survivors — any of these. The file's assessment is that she has the resources to absorb one more such loss with degradation but not destruction; two in close succession would likely push her into a depressive contraction the prior trauma did not produce.
- **Father's death with the conversation unhad.** Predicted to occur on a five-to-fifteen-year horizon. If it precedes the integration work, it forecloses a piece of the work permanently and would likely produce a year-plus depressive episode with substance use relapse risk.
- **A public failure in the courtroom register.** Disbarment proceedings, a high-profile case lost in a way that her opposition frames as gamma-form-related, a malpractice action — anything that destabilizes the legal identity she uses as fortification. Her vocational self is load-bearing; if it cracks, the whole architecture flexes.
- **A reprise of the Starfox-class violation,** in any form — being chemically, magically, or psychologically manipulated in a way that touches consent or agency. This is the injury her psyche is least equipped to absorb a second time.
- **Bruce returning in a destabilized form** — as antagonist, as victim, as someone who needs her to be the strong one before she has finished being the wounded one. This would short-circuit grief work that is still in progress.
- **A forced transformation-state change** — being trapped in human form by a power-suppression event, or trapped in gamma form by a transformation-locking attack. Either, given her form-bifurcation history, would be acutely destabilizing in ways disproportionate to the apparent stakes.
- **Slow attritional reversion.** The likeliest catastrophic vector is not a single event but the quiet substitution of overwork for life, the dropping of therapy "because she's fine now," the relationship ended for plausible reasons, the drinking reintroduced socially. No single step is alarming. The cumulative drift over twenty-four months produces the late-thirties version of her who is technically functional, professionally successful, and structurally alone in a way that has hardened into character. This is the file's primary concern, because it is the trajectory she could enter without ever noticing she had entered it.

---

### 9.7 Net Assessment

The subject is, on the integrated evidence, **more likely than not to continue integrating**. The base rates for someone with her resources — intelligence, vocation, peer network, demonstrated capacity for trauma work, a value system that organizes behavior prosocially, an integrated sense of humor — recovering from a discrete severe trauma at this point post-event are favorable. She has done the hard initial work. The remaining work is real but is the work of a person already on the road, not the work of someone who has not yet started.

The risks are not symmetric to the strengths. The strengths are durable and the risks are mostly external (second loss, antagonist action, the father's mortality) or quietly internal (the attritional drift). The file's estimate: **65-70% probability of sustained integration over the five-year horizon; 20-25% probability of reversion to a high-functioning contracted state; 5-10% probability of acute decompensation requiring extended clinical intervention, almost all of that probability concentrated in scenarios where two or more catastrophic vectors fire in close succession.**

The single intervention with the highest expected value for her long-term trajectory is continuity of therapy through the next eighteen to twenty-four months. The single behavioral indicator with the highest predictive value is the human-form occupancy rate over the same window. The single relational indicator is whether she initiates contact with her father on her own terms before he forces the issue by dying.

She is, on the long view, one of the better candidates in her cohort for what a mature, integrated, prosocial superhuman life actually looks like. The file's posture toward her is, accordingly, watchful, hopeful, and — to a degree it permits itself with few subjects — protective.

— END SECTION 9 —
